śilājālaiḥ samucchritaḥ dvīpasya tasya pūrvarddhe citrasānuḥ sthito mahān  BndP sa maṇḍalasahasrāṇi vistīrṇaḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ urddhaṃ caiva catustriṃśatsahasrāṇi mahītalāt  BndP dvīpardhasya parikṣiptaḥ parvato mānasottaraḥ sthito velāsamīpe tu navacandra ivoditaḥ  BndP yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi ūrdhvaṃ pañcāśaducchritaḥ tāvadeva ca vistīrṇaḥ sarvataḥ parimaṇḍalaḥ  BndP sa eva dvīpapaścārddhe mānasaḥ pṛthivīdharaḥ eka eva mahāsāraḥ sanniveśo dvidhā kṛtaḥ  BndP svādūdakenodadhinā sarvataḥ parivāritaḥ puṣkaradvīpavistārādvistīrṇo sau samantataḥ  BndP tasmindvīpe smṛtau dvau tu puṇyau janapadau sukhabāhulyā mānasīṃ siddhimāsthitāḥ  BndP masasāyuśca rūpaṃ ca tasminvarṣadvaye smṛtam adhamottamā na teṣvasti tulyāste rūpaśīlataḥ  BndP na tatra dasyurdamako nerṣyāsūyā bhayaṃ tathā nigraho na ca jarākramavivarjitaḥ  BndP ityeṣa dhātakīkhaṇḍe mahā vīte tathaiva ca ānupūrvyādvidhiḥ kṛtsnaḥ puṣkarasya prakīrttitaḥ  BndP svādūdakenodadhinā puṣkaraḥ parivāritaḥ vistārānmaṇḍalāccaiva puṣkarasya samena tu  BndP evaṃ dvīpāḥ samudraistu sapta saptabhirāvṛtāḥ dvīpasyānantaro yastu sāmudrastatsamastu saḥ  BndP evaṃ dvīpasamudrāṇāṃ vṛddhirjñeyā parasparāt apāṃ caiva samudrekātsāmudra iti saṃjñitaḥ  BndP viśantirnivasaṃtyasminprajā yasmāccaturvidhāḥ tasmādvarṣamiti proktaṃ prajānāṃ sukhadaṃ yataḥ  BndP ṛṣa ityeṣa ramaṇe vṛṣaśaktiprabandhane ratiprabadhanātmiddhaṃ varṣaṃ tatteṣu tena vai  BndP śuklapakṣe candravṛddhyā samudraḥ pūryate sadā prakṣīyamāṇe bahule kṣīyate stamite khage  BndP āpūryamāṇo hyudadhiḥ svata evābhipūryate tathopakṣīyamāṇe pi svātmanyevāvakṛṣyate  BndP udakasyāyanaṃ yasmāttasmādudadhirucyate aparvāṇastu girayaḥ parvabhiḥ parvatāḥ smṛtāḥ  BndP plakṣadvīpe tu gomedaḥ parvatastena caucyate śālmaliḥ śālmale dvīpe pūjyate sumahāvrataiḥ  BndP kuśadvīpe jaṃbūdvīpātpravarttante ratnāni vividhāni ca dvīpeṣu teṣu sarveṣu prajānāṃ kramatastu vai  BndP sarvaśo brahmavaryeṇa satyena ca damena ca ārogyayuḥpramāṇābhyāṃ pramāṇaṃ dviguṇaṃ tataḥ  BndP bāhyato ghanato yasya tiryagūrddhvaṃ tu maṇḍalam  BndP dhāryamāṇaṃ samantāttu tiṣṭhate yattu tejasā ayoguḍanibho vāhnaḥ samantā nmaṇḍalākṛtiḥ  BndP samantāddhanavātena dhāryamāṇaḥ sa tiṣṭhati ghanavātaṃ tathākāśo dadhānaḥ khalu tiṣṭhati  BndP bhūtādiśca tathā kāśaṃ bhūtādiścāpyasau mahān mahāśca so pyanantena hyavyaktena tu dhāryate  BndP anantamaparivyaktaṃ daśadhā sūkṣmameva ca anantama kṛtātmānamanādinidhanaṃ ca yat  BndP anityaṃ parato ghoramanālaṃbamanāmayam naikayojanasāhasraṃ viprakṛṣṭamanāvṛtam  BndP tama eva nirālokamamaryyādamadaiśikam devānāmapyaviditaṃ vyavahāravivarjitam  BndP tamasoṃte ca viśyātamākāśānte hyabhāsvaram maryādāyāmanantasya devasyāyatanaṃ mahat  BndP tridaśānāmagamyaṃ tatasthānaṃ divyamiti śrutiḥ mahato devadevasya maryādā yā vyavasthitāḥ  BndP candrādityāvadhastāttu ye lokāḥ prathitā budhaiḥ te lokā ityabhihitā jagatasca na saṃśayaḥ  BndP rasātalatalāḥ saptasaptaivorddhvatalāśca ye saptaskandhastathā vāyoḥ sabrahmasadanā dvijāḥ  BndP āpātālāddivaṃ yāvadatra pañcavidhā gatiḥ pramāṇametajjagata eṣa saṃsārasāgaraḥ  BndP anādyantāṃ vrajantyeva naikajātisamudbhavāḥ vicitrā jagataḥ sā vai prakṛtirbrahmaṇaḥ sthitā  BndP yaccaiha daivikaṃ vātha nisargaṃ bahuvistaraḥ atīndriyermahābhāgaiḥ siddhairapi na lakṣitaḥ  BndP pṛthivyaṃbvagnivāyūnāṃ nabhasastamasastathā mānasasya tu dehasya anantasya dvijottamāḥ  BndP kṣayo vā pariṇāmo vā anto vāpi na vidyate ananta eṣa sarvatra evaṃ jñāneṣu paṭhyate  BndP tasya coktaṃ mayā pūrva tasminnāmānukīrtane yaḥ padmanābhanāmnā tu tatkārtsnyena ca kīrttitaḥ  BndP sa eva sarvatra gataḥ sarvasthāneṣu pūjyate bhūmau rasātale caiva ākāśe pavane nale  BndP arṇaveṣu ca sarveṣu divi caiva na saṃśayaḥ tathā tamasi vijñeya eṣa eva mahādyutiḥ  BndP anekadhā vibhaktāṅgo mahāyogī janārdanaḥ sarvalokeṣu lokeśa ijyate bahudhā prabhuḥ  BndP evaṃ parasparotpanna dhāryante ca parasparam ādhārādheyabhāvena vikārāste vikāriṇaḥ  BndP pṛthvyādayo vikārāste paricchinnāḥ parasparam parasparadhikāścaiva praviṣṭāste parasparam  BndP yasmātsṛṣaṭāstu te nyonyaṃ tasmātsthairyamupāgatāḥ prāgāsannaviśeṣāstu viśeṣo nyaviśeṣaṇāt  BndP pṛthivyādyāstu vādyantāparicchinnāstrayastu te guṇopacayasāreṇa paricchedo viśeṣataḥ  BndP śeṣāṇāṃ tu paricchedaḥ saukṣmyānneha vibhāvyate bhūtebhyaḥ paratastebhyo vyālokā sā dharā smṛtā  BndP bhūtānyāloka ākāśe paricchinnāni sarvaśaḥ pātre mahati pātrāṇi yathaivāntargatāni tu  BndP bhavantyanyonyahīnāni parasparasamāśrayāt tathā hyāloka ākāśe bhedāstvantargatā matāḥ  BndP kṛttnānyetāni catvāri hyanyonyasyādhikāni tu yāvadetāni bhūtāni tāvadutpattirucyate  BndP tantunāmiva saṃtāro bhūteṣvantargato mataḥ pratyā khyāya tu bhūtāni kāryotparttina vidyate  BndP tasmātparimitā bhedāḥ smṛtāḥ kāryyātmakāstu te kāraṇātmakāstathaika syurbhedā ye mahadādayaḥ  BndP ityeṣa saṃniveśo vai mayā prokto vibhāgaśaḥ saptadvīpasamudrāḍyo yāthātathyana vai dvijāḥ  BndP vistarānmaṇḍalāścaiva prasaṃkhyānena caiva hi vaiśvarūpradhānasya pariṇāmaikadeśikaḥ  BndP adhiṣṭhitaṃ bhagavatā yasya sarvamidaṃ jagat evaṃbhūtagaṇāḥ sapta sanniviṣṭāḥ parasparam  BndP etāvānsaṃniveśastu mayā śakyaḥ prabhāṣitum etāvadeva śrotavyaṃ saṃniveśe tu pārtheve  BndP sapta prakṛtayastvetā dhārayanti parasparam tāstvahaṃ parimāṇena naṃ saṃkhyātumihotsahe  BndP asaṃkhyātāḥ prakṛtayastiryyagūrddhvamadhastathā tārakāsaṃniveśaśca yāvaddivyānumaṇḍalam  BndP paryyā yasanniveśastu bhūmestadanu maṇḍalaḥ ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi kṛthivyā vai vicakṣaṇāḥ  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte pūrvabhāge dvitīye nuṣaṅgapāde plakṣādidvīpavarṇanaṃ nāmaikonaviṃśatitamo dhyāyaḥsūta uvācaadhaḥpramāṇamūrddhva ca vakṣyamāṇaṃ nibodhata pṛthivī vāyurākāśamāpo jyotiśca pañcamam  BndP anantā dhātavo hyetaṃ vyāpakāstu prakīrttitāḥ jananī sarvabhūtānāṃ sarvasattvadharā dharā  BndP nānājanapadākīrṇā nānādhiṣṭhānapattanā nānānadanadīśailā naikajātisamākulā  BndP anantā gīyate devī pṛthivī bahuvistarā nadīnadasasudrasthāstanthā kṣudrāśrayasthitāḥ  BndP parvatākāśasaṃsthāśca antarbhūmigātāśca yāḥ āpo nantā hi vijñeyāstathāgniḥ sarvalokagaḥ  BndP anantaḥ paṭhyate caiva vyāpakaḥ sarvasaṃbhavaḥ tathākāśamanālekhyaṃ ramyaṃ nānāśrayaṃ smṛtam  BndP anantaṃ paṭhyate caiva vāyuścākāśasambhavaḥ āpaḥ pṛthivyāmudake pṛthivyupari saṃsthitāḥ  BndP ākāśaścāparamatha punarbhūmiḥ punarjalam evaṃ matamanantasya bhautikasya na vidyate  BndP parasparaiḥ sopacitā bhūmiścaiva nibodhata bhūmirjalamathā kāśamiti yā yā paraṃparā  BndP sthitireṣā tu vikhyātā saptame sminnasātale daśayojanasāhasramekaṃ bhaumaṃ rasātalam  BndP sādhubhiḥ parisaṃkhyātamekaikenaiva vistaram prathamaṃ tatvalaṃ nāma sutalaṃ tu tataḥ param  BndP tatastalātalaṃ vidyādatalaṃ bahuvistaram tatorvākca talaṃ nāma parataśca rasātalam  BndP eteṣāmapyadhobhāge pātālaṃ saptamaṃ smṛtam kṛṣṇabhaumaśca prathamo bhūmibhāgaḥ prakīrttitaḥ  BndP pāṇḍubhūmirdvitīyastu tṛtīyo nīlamṛttikaḥ pītabhaumaścaturthastu pañcamaḥ śarkarāmayaḥ  BndP ṣaṣṭhaḥ śilāmayo jñeyaḥ sauvarṇaḥ saptamaḥ smṛtaḥ prathame smiṃstale khyātamasuredrasya mandiram  BndP namucerindraśatrośca mahānādasya cālayam puraṃ ca śaṅkukarṇasya kabandhasya ca mandiram  BndP niṣkulādasya ca puraṃ prahṛṣṭajanasaṃkulam rākṣasasya ca bhīmasya śūladantasya cālayam  BndP lohitākṣakaliṅgānāṃ nagaraṃ śvāpadasya ca dhanañjayasya ca puraṃ nāgendrasya mahātmanaḥ  BndP kāliyasya ca nāgasya nagaraṃ kauśikasya ca evaṃ purasahasrāṇi nāgadānavarakṣasām  BndP tale jñeyāni prathame kṛṣṇabhaume na saṃśayaḥ dvitīye sutale viprā daityendrasya ca rakṣasaḥ  BndP mahājaṃbhasya tu tathā nagaraṃ prathamasya tu iyagrīvasya kṛṣṇasya nikumbhasya ca mandiram  BndP śaṅkhakhyasya ca daityasya nagaraṃ gomukhasya ca rākṣasasya ca nīlasya meghasya kathanasya ca  BndP ālayaṃ kukupādasya mahoṣṇīṣasya cālayam kaṃbalasya ca nāgasya puramaśvatarasya ca  BndP kadrūputrasya ca puraṃ takṣakasya mahātmanaḥ evaṃ purasahasrāṇi nāgadānavarakṣasām  BndP dvitīye smin tale viprāḥ pāṇḍubhaume na saṃśayaḥ tṛtīye tu tale khyātaṃ prahlādasya mahātmanaḥ  BndP anudrādasya ca puraṃ puramagnimukhasya ca tārakāśyasya ca puraṃ puraṃ triśirasastathā  BndP śiśumārasya ca puraṃ tripurasya tathā puram purañjanasya daityasya hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanākulam  BndP cyavanasya tu vijñeyaṃ rākṣasasya ca mandiram rākṣaseṃdrasya ca puraṃ kumbhilasya kharasya ca  BndP virādhasya ca krūrasya puramulkāsukhasya ca hemakasya ca nāgasya tathā pāṇḍurakasya ca  BndP maṇināgasya ca puraṃ kapilasya ca mandiram nedakasyoragapatorviśālākṣasya mandiram  BndP evaṃ purasahasrāṇi nāgadānavarakṣasām tṛtīye smiṃstale viprā nīlabhaume na saṃśayaḥ  BndP caturthe daityasiṃhasya kālanemermahātmanaḥ gajakarṇasya ca puraṃ nagaraṃ kuñjarasya ca  BndP rākṣaseṃdrasya ca puraṃ sumālerbahuvistaram muñjasya lokanāthasya vṛkavaktrasya cālayam  BndP bahuyojanavistīrṇaṃ bahupakṣisamākulam nagalaṃ vainateyasya caturthe sminnasātale  BndP pañcame śarkarābhaume bahuyojanavistaram virojanasya nagaraṃ daityasiṃhasya dhīmataḥ  BndP vaidyutasyāgniji hvasya hiraṇyākṣasya cālayam puraṃ ca vidyujjihvasya rākṣasendrasya dhīmataḥ  BndP sahāmeghasya ca puraṃ rākṣaseṃdrasya mālinaḥ kirmīrasya ca nāgasya svastikasya jayasya ca  BndP evaṃ purasahasrāṇi nāgadānavarakṣasām pañcame smiṃstale jñeyaṃ śarkarānicaye sadā  BndP ṣaṣṭhe tale daityapateḥ kesare nagarottamam suparvaṇaḥ pulomnaśca nagaraṃ mahiṣasya ca  BndP rākṣaseṃdrasya ca puraṃ suroṣasya mahātmanaḥ tatrāste suramāputraḥ śataśīrṣo mudā yutaḥ  BndP mahendrasya sakhā śrīmānvāsukināma nāgarāṭ evaṃ purasahasrāṇi nāgadānavarakṣasām  BndP ṣaṣṭhe tale sminvikhyāte śilābhaume rasātale saptame tu tale jñeyaṃ pātāle sarvapaścime  BndP puraṃ baleḥ pramuditaṃ naranā rīgaṇākulam asurāśīviṣaiḥ pūrṇaṃ sukhitairdevaśatrubhiḥ  BndP mucukundasya detyasya tatraiva nagaraṃ mahāt anekairditiputrāṇāṃ samudīrṇairmahāpuraiḥ  BndP tathaiva nāganagarairdyutimadbhiḥ sahasraśaḥ daityānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca samudīrṇairmahāpuraiḥ  BndP udīrṇai rākṣasāvāsairanekaiśca samākulam pātālānte ca viprendrā vistīṇa bahuyojane  BndP āste raktāravindākṣo mahātmā hyajarāmaraḥ dhautaśaṅkhodaravapurnīla vāsā mahābalaḥ  BndP viśālabhogo dyutimāṃścitramālyadharo balī rukmaśṛṅgāvadātena dīptāsyena virājatā  BndP prabhurmukha sahasreṇa śobhate caikakuṇḍalī sa jihvāmālayā dīpto lolajjvālānalārciṣā  BndP jvālāmālāparikṣiptaḥ kailāsa iva lakṣya te sa tu netrasahasreṇa dviguṇena virājatā  BndP bālasūryābhitāmreṇa śarīrasnigdhapāṇḍunā tasya kundenduvarṇasya netramālā virājate  BndP taruṇādityamāleva śvetaparvatamūrddhani vikarālocchritatanurlakṣyate śayanāsane  BndP vistīrṇa iva medinyāṃ sahasraśikharo giriḥ mahānāgairmahābhogairmahāvijñairmahātmabhiḥ  BndP upāsyate mahātejā mahānāgapatiḥ svayam sa rājā sarvanāgānāṃ śeṣo nanto mahādyutiḥ  BndP sā vaiṣṇavī vyavahṛtirmaryādā yā vyavasthitā saptaivamete kathitā vyavahāryā rasātalāḥ  BndP devāsurama hānāgarākṣasādhyuṣitāḥ sadā ataḥ paramanālokamagamyaṃ siddhasādhubhiḥ  BndP devānāmapyaviditaṃ vyavahāravivakṣayā pṛthvyaṃbuva ṅnivāyūnāṃ nabhasaśca dvijottamāḥ  BndP mahattvamṛṣibhiścaivaṃ varṇyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi sūryācandramasorgatim  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte pūrvabhāgedvitīye nuṣaṅgapāde dholokavarṇanaṃ nāma viṃśatitamo dhyāyaḥsūta uvācasūryā candramasāvetau bhramato yāvadeva tu prakāśaistu prabhābhistau maṇḍalābhyāṃ samucchritau  BndP saptānāṃ tu samudrāṇāṃ dvīpānāṃ satu vistaraḥ vistarārddhe pṛthivyāstu bhavedanyatra bāhyataḥ  BndP paryāsaparimāṇaṃ tu candrādityau prakāśataḥ paryāstātpārimāṇyena bhūmestulyaṃ divaṃ smṛtam  BndP avati trīnimāṃllokān yasmātsūryaḥ paribhraman avidhātuḥ prakāśākhyo hyavanātsa raviḥ smṛtaḥ  BndP ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi pramāṇaṃ candrasūryayoḥ mahittattvānmahīśabdo hyasminvarṣe nipādyate  BndP asya bhāratavarṣasya viṣkaṃbhāttulyavistṛtam maṇḍalaṃ bhāskarasyātha yojanāni nibodhata  BndP navayojanasāhasro vistāro bhāskarasya tu vistārātrriguṇaścāsya pariṇāhastu maṇḍale  BndP viṣkaṃbhamaṇḍalāccaiva bhāskarāddviguṇaḥ śaśī atha pṛthivyā vakṣyāmi pramāṇaṃ yojanaiḥ saha  BndP saptadvīpasamudrāyā vistāro maṇḍalaṃ ca yat ityetadiha saṃkhyātaṃ purāṇe parimāṇataḥ  BndP tadvakṣyāmi samākhyāya sāṃpratairabhimānibhiḥ abhimāninovyatītā ye tulyāste sāṃprataistviha  BndP devā ye vai vyatītāstu rūpairnāmabhireva ca tasmāttu sāṃpratairdevairvakṣyāmi vasudhātalam  BndP divāstu sanniveśaṃ vai sāṃprataireva kṛtsnaśaḥ śatārddhakoṭivistārā pṛthivī kṛtsnaśaḥ smṛtā  BndP tasyā ūrddhvapramāṇena meroryāvattu saṃsthitiḥ pṛthivyā hyarddhavistāro yojanāgrātprakīrttitaḥ  BndP merormadhyātpratidiśaṃ koṭirekā tu sā smṛtā tathā śātasahasrāṇāmekona navatiḥ punaḥ  BndP pañcāśattu sahasrāṇi pṛthivyarddhasya maṇḍalam gaṇitaṃ yojanāgrāttu koṭyastvekādaśa smṛtāḥ  BndP tathā śatasahasrāṇi saptatriṃśādhikāni tu ityetadiha saṃśyātaṃ pṛthivyantasya maṇḍalam  BndP tārakāsaṃniveśāsya divi yāva cca maṇḍalam paryāsasanniveśaśca bhūmeryāvattu maṇḍalam  BndP paryāsaparimāṇena bhūmestulyaṃ divaḥ smṛtam saptānāmapi dvīpānāmeta tsthānaṃ prakīrtitam  BndP paryāyaparimāṇena maṇḍalānugatena ca uparyupari lokānāṃ chatravatparimaṇḍalam  BndP saṃsthitirvihitā sarvā yeṣu tiṣṭhanti jantavaḥ etadaṇḍakapālasya pramāṇaṃ parikīrttitam  BndP aṇḍasyāntastvime lokāḥ saptadvīpā ca medinī bhūrlokaśca bhuvarllokastṛtīyassṛriti ssvataḥ  BndP maharlloko janaścaiva tapaḥ satyaṃ ca saptamam ete sapta kṛtā lokāśchatrākārā vyavasthitāḥ  BndP svakairāvaraṇaiḥ sūkṣmairdhāryamāṇāḥ pṛthakpṛthak daśabhāgādhikābhiśca tābhiḥ prakṛtibhirbahiḥ  BndP pūryamāṇā viśeṣaiśca samutpannaiḥ parasparāt asyāṇḍasya samantācca sanniviṣṭo ghanodadhiḥ  BndP pṛthivyā maṇḍalaṃ kṛtsnaṃ ghanatoyena dhāryate ghanodadhiḥ pareṇātha dhāryyate ghanatejasā  BndP bāhyato ghanatejasca tiryyagūrddhvaṃ tu maṇḍalam saṃmatāddhanavātena dhāryamāṇaṃ pratiṣṭhitam  BndP ghanavātaṃ tathākāśamākāśaṃ ca mahātmanā bhūtādinā vṛtaṃ sarvaṃ bhūtādirmahatā vṛtaḥ  BndP vṛto mahānanantena pradhānenāvya yātmanā purāṇi lokapālānāṃ pravakṣyāmi yathākramam  BndP jyotirguṇapracārasya pramāṇaparisiddhaye meroḥ prācyāṃ diśi tathā mānasasyaiva mūrddhani  BndP vasvaukasārā māhendrī purī hemapariṣkṛtā dakṣiṇena punarmerormānasasyaiva mūrddhani  BndP vaivasvato niva sati yamaḥ saṃyamane pure pratīcyāṃ tu punarmerormānasasyaiva mūrddhani  BndP sukhā nāma purī ramyā varuṇasyāpi dhīmataḥ varuṇo yādasāṃ nāthassukhākhye vasate pure  BndP diśyuttarasyāṃ merostu mānasasyaiva mūrddhani tulyā mahendrapuryyāstu somasyāpi vibhāvarī  BndP mānasottaravṛṣṭe tu lokapālāścaturdiśam sthitā dharmavyavasthārtha lokamaṃrakṣaṇāya ca  BndP lokapālopariṣṭāttu sarvato dakṣiṇāyane kāṣṭhāgatasya sūryasya gatiyā tāṃ nibodhata  BndP dakṣiṇo pakrame sūryyaḥ kṣipteṣuriva sarpati jyotiṣāṃ cakramādāya satataṃ parigacchati  BndP madhyagaścāmarāvatyāṃ yadā bhavati bhāskaraḥ vaivasvate saṃyamate udayastatra dṛśyate  BndP sukhāyāmarddharātraṃ syādvibhāyāmastameti ca vaivasvate saṃyamane madhyagaḥ syādraviryadā sukhāyāmatha vāruṇyāmuttiṣṭhansa tu dṛśyate  BndP vibhāyā marddharātraṃ syānmāhendyāmastameti ca yadā dakṣiṇapurveṣāmaparāhṇo vidhīyate  BndP dakṣiṇāparadeśyānāṃ pūrvahṇaḥ parikī rttitaḥ teṣāmapararātraśca ye janā uttarāḥ pare  BndP deśā uttarapūrvā ye pūvarātrastu tānprati evamevottareṣvar ke bhuvaneṣu virājate  BndP sukhāyāsatha vāruṇyāṃ madhyāhne cāryamā yadā vibhāyāṃ somapuryāṃ vā uttiṣṭhati vibhāvasuḥ  BndP rātryarddha cāmarāvatyāmastameti yamasya ca somapuryā vibhāyāṃ tu madhyāhne syāddivākaraḥ  BndP mahedrasyāmarāvatyāṃ sūrya uttiṣṭhate tadā arddharātraṃ saṃyamane vāruṇyāmastameti ca  BndP sa śīghrameva paryeti bhāskaro lātaca travat bhramanvai bhramamārṇāni ṛkṣāṇi carate raviḥ  BndP evaṃ caturṣu pārśveṣu dakṣiṇāṃ tena sarpati udayāstamane cāsāvṛtti ṣṭhati punaḥ punaḥ  BndP pūvāhṇe cāparāhṇe ca dvau dvau devālayau tu saḥ tapatyarkaśca madhyāhne taireva ca svaraśmibhiḥ  BndP udito varddhamānābhirāmadhyāhnaṃ tapanraviḥ ataḥ paraṃ hrasaṃtībhirgobhirastaṃ nigacchati  BndP udayāstamayābhyāṃ ca smṛte pūrvāpare diśau yāvatpurastāttapati tāpatpṛṣṭhe tha pārśvayoḥ  BndP yatrodyandṛśyate sūryasteṣāṃ sa udayaḥ samṛtaḥ praṇāśaṃ gacchate yatra teṣāmastaḥ sa ucyate  BndP sarveṣāmuttare meruloṅkālokaśca dakṣiṇe vidūrabhāvādarkasya bhūmilekhāvṛtasya ca  BndP līyante raśmayo BndP uttaraprakrame cāpi divā mandā gatistathā tathaiva ca punarnaktaṃ śīghrā sūryasya vai gātiḥ  BndP dakṣiṇaprakrameṇaiva divā śīghraṃ vidhīyate gatiḥ sūryasya naktaṃ ca mandā caiva gatistathā  BndP śaiśumāre vyavasthitaḥ uttānapādaputro sau meḍhībhūto dhruvo divi  BndP sa vai bhrāmayate nityaṃ candrādityau grahaiḥ saha bhramantamanugacchanti nakṣatrāṇi ca cakravat  BndP dhruvasya manasā cāsau sarvate jyotiṣāṃ gaṇaḥ sūryācandramasau tārā nakṣatrāṇi grahaiḥ saha  BndP vātānīkamayairbandhairdhruve baddhāni tāni vai teṣāṃ yogaśca bhedaśca kālaścārastathaiva ca  BndP astodayau tathotpātā ayane dakṣaṇottare viṣuvadgrahavarṇāśca druvātsarvaṃ pravarttate  BndP varṣā gharmo himaṃ rātriḥ saṃdhyā caiva dinaṃ tathā śubhāśubhaṃ prajānāṃ ca dhruvātsarvaṃ pravarttate  BndP dhruveṇādhiṣṭitaścaiva sūryo po gṛhya varṣati tadeṣa dīpta kiraṇaḥ sa kālagnirdivākaraḥ  BndP parivarttakramādviprā bhābhirālokayan diśaḥ sūryaḥ kiramajālena vāyuyuktena sarvaśaḥ  BndP jagato jalamādatte kṛtsnasya dvijasattamāḥ ādityapītaṃ sakalaṃ somaḥ saṃkramate jalam  BndP nāḍībhirvāyuyuktābhirlokadhārā pravarttate yatsomātsravate hyaṃbu tadanneṣveva tiṣṭhati  BndP meghā vāyuvighātena visṛjanti jalaṃ bhūvi evamutkṣipyate caiva patate cāsakṛjjalam  BndP na nāśa udakasyāsti tadeva parivarttate saṃdhāraṇārthaṃ lokānāṃ māyaiṣā viśvanirmitā  BndP anyā māyayā vyāptaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram viśveśo lokakṛddevaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ  BndP dhātā kṛtsnasya lokasya prabhaviṣṇurdivākaraḥ sārvalokikamaṃbho yattatsomānnabhasaśvyutam  BndP somādhāraṃ jagatsarvametattathyaṃ prakīrtitam sūryāduṣṇaṃ nisravate somācchītaṃ pravarttate  BndP śītoṣṇavīryauṃ dvāvetau yuktyā dhārayato jagat somādhārā nadī gaṅgā pavitrā vimalodakā  BndP bhadrasomapurogāśca mahānadyo dvijottamāḥ sarvabhūtaśarīreṣu hyāpo hyanusṛtāśca yāḥ  BndP teṣu saṃdahyamāneṣu jaṅgamasthāvareṣu ca dhūmabhūtāstu tā hyāpo niṣkāmantīha sarvaśaḥ  BndP tena cābhrāṇi jāyante sthānamabhramayaṃ smṛtam tejorkaḥ sarvabhūtebhya ādatte raśmibhirjalam  BndP samudrādvāyusaṃyogādvahantyāpo gabhastayaḥ saṃjīvanaṃ ca sasyānāmaṃbhastadamṛtopamam  BndP tatastvṛtuvaśātkāle parivatya divākaraḥ yacchatyāpo hi meghebhyaḥ ghuklāśuklairgabhastibhiḥ  BndP abhrasthāḥ prapatantyāpo vāyunā samudīritāḥ sarvabhūtahitārthāya vāyumiśrāḥ samantataḥ  BndP tato varṣati ṣaṇmāsānsarvabhūtavivṛddhaye vāyavyaṃ stanitaṃ caiva vaidyutaṃ cāgnisaṃbhavam  BndP mehanācca mihedhātomaghatvaṃ vyajayanti hi na bhraśyanti yataścāpastadabhaṃ kavayo viduḥ  BndP meghānāṃ punarutpattiśtrividhā yonirucyate āgneyā brahmajāścaiva pakṣajāśca pṛthagvidhāḥ  BndP tridhā meghāḥ samākhyātāsteṣāṃ vakṣyāmi saṃbhavam āgneyā stūṣṇajāḥ proktāsteṣāṃ dhūmapravarttanam  BndP śītadurdinavātā ye svaguṇāste vyavasthitāḥ mahiṣāśca vārāhāśca mattamātaṅgarūpiṇaḥ  BndP bhūtvā dharaṇimabhyetya ramante vicaranti ca jīmūtā nāma te meghā hyetebhyo jīvasaṃbhavaḥ  BndP vidyudguṇavihīnāśca jaladhārā vilaṃbinaḥ mūkameghā mahākāyā āvahasya vaśānugāḥ  BndP krośamātrācca varṣanti krośārddhādapi vā punaḥ parvatāgra nitaṃbeṣu varṣati ca rasaṃti ca  BndP balākāgarbhadāścaiva balākāgarbhadhāriṇaḥ brahmajā nāma te meghā brahmaniśvāsasaṃbhavāḥ  BndP te hi vidyudguṇopetāstanayitnupriyasvanāḥ teṣāṃ śaśrvatpraṇādena bhūmiḥ svāṅgarūhodbhavā  BndP rājñī rājyābhiṣikteva punaryauṃvanamaśnute teṣviyaṃ prāvṛḍāsaktā bhūtānāṃ jīvitodbhavā  BndP dvitīyaṃ pravahaṃ vāyuṃ meghāste tu samāśritāḥ etaṃ yojanamātrācca sādhyarddhā niṣkṛtādapi  BndP vṛṣṭirgarbhastridhā teṣāṃ dhārāsāraḥ prakīrttitaḥ puṣkarāvarttakā nāma te meghāḥ pakṣasaṃbhavāḥ  BndP śakreṇa pakṣacchinnā ye parvatānāṃ mahaujasām kāmāgānāṃ pravṛddhānāṃ bhūtānāṃ śivamicchatā  BndP puṣkarā nāma te meghā bṛṃhantastoyamatsarāḥ puṣkarāvarttakāstena kāraṇeneha śabditāḥ  BndP nānārūpadharāścaiva mahāghorasvanāśca te kalpāntavṛṣṭeḥ sraṣṭāraḥ saṃvartāgne rniyāmakāḥ  BndP varṣantyete yugānteṣu tṛtīyāste prakīrttitāḥ anekarūpasaṃsthānāḥ pūrayanto mahītalam  BndP vāyuṃ purā vahantaḥ syurāśritāḥ kalpasādhakāḥ yānyaṇḍasya tu bhinnasya prākṛtasyābhavaṃstadā  BndP yasminbrahmā samutpannaścaturvaktraḥ svayaṃprabhuḥ tānyevāṇḍakapālāni sarve meghāḥ prakīrttitāḥ  BndP teṣāmāpyāyanaṃ dhūmaḥ sarveṣāmaviśeṣataḥ teṣāṃ śreṣṭhastu parjanyaścatvāraścaiva diggajāḥ  BndP gajānāṃ parvatānāṃ ca meghānāṃ bhogibhiḥ saha kulamekaṃ pṛthagbhūtaṃ yonirekā jalaṃ smṛtam  BndP parjanyo diggajā ścaiva hemante śītasaṃbhavāḥ tuṣāravṛṣṭiṃ varṣanti śiṣṭaḥ sasyapravṛddhaye  BndP ṣaṣṭhaḥ parivaho nāma teṣāṃ vāyurapāśrayaḥ yo sau bibartti bhagavāngaṅgāmākāśagocarām  BndP divyāmṛtajalā puṇyāṃ tridhāsvātipathe sthitām tasyā niṣyandatoyāni diggajāḥ pṛthubhiḥ karaiḥ  BndP śīkaraṃ saṃpramuñcanti nīhāra iti sa smṛtaḥ dakṣiṇena giriryo sau hemakūṭa iti smṛtaḥ  BndP udagghimavataḥ śaila uttaraprāyadakṣiṇe puṇḍraṃ nāma samākhyātaṃ nagaraṃ tatra vistṛtam  BndP tasminnipatitaṃ varṣaṃ tattuṣārasamudbhavam tatastadā vaho vāyurhemavantaṃ samudvahan  BndP ānayatyātmayogena siṃcamāno mahāgirim himavantamatikramya vṛṣṭiśeṣaṃ tataḥ param  BndP ihābhyeti tataḥ paścādaparāntavivṛddhaye varṣadvayaṃ samākhyātaṃ sasyadvayavivṛddhaye  BndP meghāścāpyāyanaṃ caiva sarvametatprakīrttitam sūrya eva tu vṛṣṭīnāṃ sraṣṭā samupadiśyate  BndP sūryamūlā ca vai vṛṣṭirjalaṃ sūryātpravartate dhruveṇādhiṣṭhitaḥ sūryastasyāṃ vṛṣṭau pravarttate  BndP dhruveṇādhiṣṭito vāyurvṛṣṭiṃ saṃharate punaḥ graho niḥsṛtya sūryāttu kṛtsne nakṣatramaṇḍale  BndP caritvānte viśatyarkaṃ dhruveṇa samādhiṣṭhitam tataḥ sūryarathasyātha sanniveśaṃ nibodhata  BndP saṃsthitenaikacakreṇa pañcāreṇa trinābhinā hiraṇmayena bhagavāṃstathaiva haridarvaṇā  BndP aṣṭāpadanibaddhena ṣaṭprakāraikaneminā cakreṇa bhāsvatā sūryaḥ syandanena prasarpati  BndP daśayojanasāhasro vistārāyāmataḥ smṛtaḥ dviguṇo sya rathopasthādīṣādaṇḍaḥ pramāṇataḥ  BndP sa tasya brahmaṇā sṛṣṭo ratho hyarthavaśena tu asaṃgaḥ kāñcano divyo yuktaḥ pavanagairhayaiḥ  BndP chandobhirvājirūpaistu yataścakraṃ tataḥ sthitaiḥ vāruṇasyandanasyeha lakṣaṇaiḥ sadṛśastu saḥ  BndP tenāsau sarvate vyomni bhāsvatā tu divākaraḥ athaitāni tu sūryasya pratyaṅgāni rathasya ha  BndP saṃvatsarasyāvayavaiḥ kalpi tasya yathākramam ahastu nābhiḥ saurasya ekacakrasya vai smṛtaḥ  BndP arāḥ pañcārttavāṃstasya nemiḥ ṣaḍṛtavaḥ smṛtaḥ rathanīḍaḥ smṛto hyeṣa cāyane kūbarāvubhau  BndP muhūrttā bandhurāstasya ramyāścāsya kalāḥ smṛtāḥ tasya kāṣṭhā smṛtā ghoṇā akṣadaṇḍaḥ kṣaṇastu vai  BndP nimeṣaścānukarṣo sya hīṣā cāsya lavāḥsmṛtāḥ rātrirvarūtho dharmo sya dhvaja ūrddhva samucchritaḥ  BndP yugākṣakoḍī te tasya arthakāmāvubhau smṛtau saptāśvarūpāśchandāsi vahanto vāmato dhuram  BndP gāyatrī caiva triṣṭupya hyanuṣṭubjagatī tathā paṅktiśca bṛhatī caiva hyuṣṇikcaiva tu saptamī  BndP cakramakṣe nibaddhaṃ tu dhruve cākṣaḥ samarpitaḥ sahacakro bhramatyakṣaḥ sahakṣo bhramate dhruvaḥ  BndP akṣeṇa saha cakreśo bhramate sau dhruveritaḥ evamarthavaśāttasya sanniveśo rathasya tu  BndP tathā saṃyogabhāvena saṃsiddho bhāsuro rathaḥ tenāsau taraṇirdevo bhāsvatā sarpate divi  BndP yugākṣakoṭisannaddhau dvau raśmī syandanasya tu dhruve tau bhrāmyate raśmī ca cakrayugayostu vai  BndP bhramato maṇḍalānyasya khecarasya rathasya tu yugākṣakoṭī te tasya dakṣiṇe syandanasya hi  BndP dhruveṇa pragṛhīte vai vicakrama turakṣavat bhramantamanugacchetāṃ dhruvaṃ raśmī tu tāvubhau  BndP yugākṣakoṭistattasya raśmibhiḥ syandanasya tu kīlāsaktā yathā rajjurbhraṃmate sarvato diśam  BndP hrasatastasya raśmī tu maṇḍaleṣūttarāyaṇe varddhate dakṣiṇe caiva bhramato maṇḍalāni tu  BndP yugākṣakoṭisaṃbaddhau raśmī dvau syandanasya tu dhruveṇa pragṛhītau vai tau raśmī nayato ravim  BndP ākṛṣyete yadā tau vai dhruveṇa sama dhiṣṭhitau tadā so bhyantare sūryo bhramate maṇḍalāni tu  BndP aśītirmaṇḍalaśataṃ kāṣṭhayorantaraṃ smṛtam dhruveṇa mucyamānābhyāṃ raśmibhyāṃ punareva tu  BndP tathaiva bāhyataḥ sūryo bhramate maṇḍalāni tu udveṣāṭayansa vegena maṇḍalāni tu gacchati  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte pūrvabhāge dvitīye nuṣaṅgapāde devagrahānukīrtanaṃ nāma dvāviṃśatitamo dhyāyaḥsūta uvācasaratho dhiṣṭhito devairādityairmunibhistathā gandharvairapsarobhiśca grāmaṇīsarparākṣasaiḥ  BndP ete vasaṃti vai sūrye dvau dvau māsau krameṇa tu dhātāryamā pulastyaśca pulahaśca prajāpatiḥ  BndP erāvato vāsukiśca kaṃso bhīmaśca tāvubhau rathakṛcca rathaujāśca yakṣāvetāvudā tdṛtau  BndP tuṃbururnāradaścaiva susthalā puñjikasthalā rakṣo hetiḥ prahetiśca yātudhānāvudāhṛtau  BndP ete vasaṃti vai sūryye madhumādhavayoḥ sadā mitraśca varuṇaścaiva muniratrirudāhṛtaḥ  BndP tathā vasiṣṭho vikhyātaḥ sahajanyā ca menakā rākṣasau ca samākhyātau pauruṣeyo vadhastathā  BndP hāhā hūhūśca gandharvauṃ yajñaścāpi rathasvanaḥ rathacitrastathaivānyo nāgasākṣakasaṃjñetaḥ  BndP raṃbhakaśca vasantyete māsayoḥ śuciśukrayoḥ tataḥ sūrye punastvanyā nivasaṃtīha devatāḥ  BndP idraścaiva vivasvāṃśca aṅgirā bhṛgureva ca elāpatrastathā sarpaḥ śaṅkhapālāśca tāvubhau  BndP viśvāvasūgrasenau ca śvetaścaivāruṇastathā pramlocā iti vikhyātānumloceti ca te ubhe  BndP yātudhānastadā sarpo vyāghraścava tu tāvubhau nabhonabhasyayoreṣa gāṇo vasati bhāskare  BndP śaradyanyāḥ punaḥ śubhrā vasaṃti munidevatāḥparjanyaścaiva pūṣā ca bhāradvājaḥ sagautamaḥ  BndP parāvasuśca gandharvastathaiva suruciśca yaḥ viśvācī ca ghṛtācī ca ubhe te śubhalakṣaṇe  BndP nāga erāvataścaiva viśrutaśca dhanañjayaḥ ścenajicca suṣeṇaśca senīrgrāma ṇīśca tau  BndP āpo vātaśca dvāvetau yātudhānāvudāhṛtau vasaṃtyete tu vai sūrye sadaivāśvinakartike  BndP haimantikau tu dvau māsau vasaṃti ca divākare aṃśo bhagaśca dvāvaitau kaśyapaśya kratuśca ha  BndP bhujaṅgaśca mahāpadmaḥ sarvaḥ karkeṭaka stathā citrasenaśca gandharva ūrṇāyuścaiva tāvubhau  BndP urvaśī pūrvacittiśca tathaivāpsarasā ubhe tārkṣaścāriṣṭanemiśca senānīr grāmaṇīśca tau  BndP vidyutsphūrjaḥ śatāyuśca yātudhānāvudātdṛtau sahe caiva sahasye ca vasaṃtyete divākare  BndP tataḥ śaiśira yoścāpi māsayornivasaṃti vai tvaṣṭā viṣṇurjāmadagnyo viśvāmitrastathaiva ca  BndP kādraveyau tathā nāgau kaṃbalāśvatarāvubhau gandharvo dhṛtarāṣṭraśca sūryavarcāstathaiva ca  BndP tilottamā tathā raṃbhā brahmāpetaśca rākṣasaḥ yajñāpetamtathaivānyo viśyāto rākṣaso ttamaḥ  BndP ṛtajitsatyajiccaiva gandharvauṃ samudāhṛtau tapastapasyayoḥ sūrye vasaṃti munisattamāḥ  BndP pitṛdevamanuṣyādīnsa sadāpyāyayanprabhuḥ parivarttatyahorātrakāraṇaṃ savitā dvijāḥ  BndP ete devā vasaṃtyarke dvau dvau māsau krameṇa tu sthānābhimānino hyete gāṇā dvādaśasaptakāḥ  BndP suryasyāpyāyayantyete tejasā teja uttamamā grathitaiḥ svairvacobhiśca stuvanti hyṛṣayo ravim  BndP gandharvāpsarasaścaiva gītanṛtyairupāsate grāmaṇīyakṣabhūtāni kurvate bhīṣusaṃgraham  BndP sarpā vahanti vai sūryaṃ yātudhānāstu yānti ca vālakhilyā naṃyatyastaṃ parivāryodayādravim  BndP eteṣāmeva devānāṃ yathāvīryaṃ yathātapaḥ yathādharmaṃ yathāyogaṃ yathāsatyaṃ yathābalam  BndP tapatyasau taśrā sūrya eṣāmindrastu tejasā ityete nivasaṃtīha dvau dvau māsau divākare  BndP ṛṣayo devagandharvāḥ pannagāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ grāmaṇyaśca tathā yakṣā yātudhānāśca mukhyaśaḥ  BndP ete tapanti varṣanti bhānti vānti sṛjanti ca bhūtānāṃ caśubhaṃ karma vyapohanti prakīrttitāḥ  BndP mānavānāṃ śubhaṃ hyete harante duritātmanām duritaṃ supracārāṇāṃ vyapohanti kvaci tkvacit  BndP ete sahaiva sūryeṇa bhramanti divāsānugāḥ varṣantaśca tapantaśca hlādayantaśca vai prajāḥ  BndP gopāyanti ca bhūtāni sarvāṇīhāmanukṣayāt sthānābhimānināmetatsthānaṃ manvantareṣu vai  BndP atītānāgatānāṃ ca varttante sāṃprataṃ ca ye evaṃ vasaṃti vai sūrye saptakāste caturdaśa caturdaśasu sarveṣu gaṇā manvantareṣviha  BndP grīṣme ca varṣāsu ca muñcamāno gharmaṃ himaṃ varṣa dinaṃ niśāṃ ca gacchatyasāvṛtuvaśātparivṛttaraśmirdevān pitṝṃśca manujāṃśca hi tarpayanvai  BndP prīṇāti devānamṛtena sūryaḥ somaṃ suṣumṇena ca varddhayitvā śukle tu pūrṇaṃ divasakrameṇa taṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe vibudhāḥ pibanti  BndP pītaṃ ca somaṃ hi kalāvaśiṣṭaṃ kṛṣṇakṣaye raśmibhirakṣarantam sudhāmṛtaṃ tatpitaraḥ pibanti devāśca saumyāśca tathaiva kāvyāḥ  BndP sūryeṇa gobhiśca samujjhitābhiradbhiḥ punaścaiva samuddhṛtābhiḥ vṛṣṭyābhivṛddhābhirathauṣadhībhirmartyāḥ kṣudhaṃ tvannapānairjayanti  BndP tṛptiśca śukle sudhayā surāṇāṃ pakṣe ca kṛṣṇe śaśvatsavitā carācaram  BndP harirharidbhirhri yate turaṅgamaiḥ pibatyathāpo haribhiḥ sahasradhā tataḥ pramuñcatyapi tāstvasau hariḥ samūhyamāno haribhisturaṅgamaiḥ  BndP ityeṣa ekacakreṇa chandobhiraśvarūpaistairyataścakraṃ tataḥ sthitaiḥ kāmarūpaiḥ sakṛdyuktairvāmatastairmanojavaiḥ  BndP haritaikhyayaiḥ piṅgairīśvarairbrahmavādibhiḥ tryaśītimaṇḍalaśataṃ bhramantyabdena te hayāḥ  BndP bāhyamābhyantaraṃ caiva maṇḍalaṃ divasakramāt kalpādau saṃpra yuktāste vahantyābhūtasaṃplavāt  BndP āvṛttā vālakhilyaiste bhramante rātryahāni tu vacobhiragryairgrathitaiḥ stūyamāno maharṣibhiḥ  BndP sevyate gītanṛtyaiśca gandharvaiścāpsarogaṇaiḥ pataṅgaiḥ patagairaśvairbhramamāṇo divaspatiḥ  BndP rathāstracakraḥsomasya kudābhāstasya vājinaḥ vāmadakṣiṇato yuktā daśa tena carantyasau  BndP vīthyāśrayāṇi ṛkṣāṇi dhruvādhāreṇa vegitāḥ hrāsavṛddhī tathaivāsya raśmīnāṃ sūryavatsmṛte  BndP tricakrobhayato śvaśca vijñeyaḥ śaśino rathaḥ apāṃ garṇātsamutpanno rathaḥ sāśvaḥ sasārathiḥ  BndP śatāraiśca tribhiścakrairyuktaḥ śuklairhayottamaiḥ daśabhistu kṛśairdivyairasaṃgaistairmanojavaiḥ  BndP sakṛdyukte rathe tāsminvahante cāyugakṣayāt saṃgṛhītarathe tasmiñśvetaścakṣuḥśravāśca vai  BndP aśvāstamekavarṇaste vahante śaṅkhavarcasaḥ yajuścaṇḍamanāścaiva vṛṣo vājī naro hayaḥ  BndP aśvo gaviṣṇurvikhyāto haṃso vyomo mṛgastathā ityete nāmabhiḥ sarve daśa candramaso hayāḥ  BndP ete candramasaṃ devaṃ vahanti saha dīkṣayā devaiḥ parivṛtaḥ somaḥ pitṛbhiścaiva gacchati  BndP somasya śuklapakṣādau bhāskare parataḥ sthire āpūryate parasyānte satataṃ divasakramāt  BndP devaiḥ pītatanuṃ somamāpyāyayati nityadā kṣīṇaṃ pañcadaśāhaṃ tu raśminaikena bhāskaraḥ  BndP āpūrayansuṣumṇena bhāgaṃ bhāgamahaḥkramāt suṣumṇāpyāyamānasya śuklā varddhanti vai kalāḥ  BndP tasmāddhrasaṃti vai kṛṣṇe śukle svāpyāyayanti tam ityevaṃ sūryavīryeṇa candraścāpyāyitastataḥ  BndP paurṇamāsyāṃ sa dṛśyeta śuklaḥ saṃpūrṇamaṇḍalaḥ evamāpyāyitaḥ somaḥ śukla pakṣe dinakramāt  BndP tato dvitīyāprabhṛti bahulasya caturddaśīm apāṃ sāramayasyendo rasamātrātmakasya tu  BndP pibatyaṃbumayaṃ devā hṛṣṭāḥ saumyaṃ svadhāmṛtam saṃbhṛtaṃ tvarddhamāsena hyamṛtaṃ sūryatejasā  BndP bhakṣārthamamṛtaṃ somaḥ paurṇamāsyāmupāsate ekāṃ rātriṃ suraiḥ sarvaiḥ pitṛbhiḥ sarṣibhiḥ saha  BndP somasya kṛṣṇapakṣādau bhāskarābhimukhasya tu prakṣīyante pidṛdevaiḥ pīyamānāḥ kalāḥ kramāt  BndP trayaśca triṃśataścaiva trayastriṃśattathaiva ca trayaśca trisahasrāśca devāḥ somaṃ pibanti vai  BndP ityetaiḥ pīyamānasya kṛṣṇā varddhati vai kalāḥ kṣīyanti tasmācchuklāśca kṛṣṇā āpyāyayanti ca  BndP evaṃ dinakramātpīte vibudhaistu niśākare pītvārddha māsaṃ gacchanti cāmāvāsyāṃ surottamāḥ  BndP pitaraścopatiṣṭhanti hyamāvāsyāṃ niśākaram tataḥ pañcadaśekāle kiñcicchiṣṭe kalātmake  BndP aparāhṇe pitṛgaṇā jaghanyaṃ payupāsate pibanti dvilavaṃ kālaṃ śiṣṭāstasya kalāstu yāḥ  BndP niḥsṛtaṃ tadamāvāsyāṃ gabhastibhyaḥ svadhāmṛtam tāṃ svadhāṃ māsatṛptyai ca pītvā gacchanti te mṛtam  BndP sūryastasminsuṣumṇe pañcābdā ye dvicaiḥ smṛtāḥ saumyāstu ṛtuvo jñeyā māsā barhiṣadaḥ smṛtāḥ  BndP agniṣvāttārttavāścaiva pitṛsargā hi vai dvijāḥ pitṛbhiḥ pīyamānasya pañcadaśyāṃ kalā tu vai  BndP yāvatprakṣīyate tasya śrīmānbhaumasyāpi rathottamaḥ asaṃgairlohitairaśvaiḥ sarvagairagnisaṃbhavaiḥ  BndP prasarpati kumāro vai ṛjuvakrānuva kragaiḥ tataścāṅgiraso vidvāndevācāryo bṛhaspatiḥ  BndP gaurairaśvaiḥ kāñcanena vātaraśmayaḥ sarvā dhruve nibaddhāśca bhramantyo bhrāmayanti tāḥ  BndP tailapīḍā yathā cakraṃ bhramanto bhrāmayanti ha tathā bhramanti jyotīṃṣi vātabaddhāni sarvaśaḥ  BndP alātacakravadyānti vātacakreritāni tu yato jyotīṃṣi vahate pravahastena sa smṛtaḥ  BndP evaṃ dhruvanibaddho sau sarpate jyotiṣāṃ gaṇaḥ saiṣa tārāmayo jñeyaḥ śiśumāro dhruvo divi  BndP yadahnā kurute pāpaṃ dṛṣṭvā tanniśimuñcate yāvatyaścaiva tārāstāḥ śiśumārāśritā divi  BndP tāvantyeva tu varṣāṇi jīvatābhyadhikāni tu sākāraḥ śiśumāraśca vijñeyaḥ pravibhāgaśaḥ  BndP auttānapādastasyātha vijñeyo hyattaro hanuḥ yajñaḥ parastu vijñeyo dharmo marddhānamāśritaḥ  BndP hṛdi nārāyaṇaḥ sādhyo hyaśvinau pūrvapādayoḥ varuṇaścāryamā caiva paścime tasya sakthinī  BndP śiśraṃ saṃvatsarastasya mitro pānaṃ samāśritaḥ pucche gniśca mahendraśca mārīcaḥ kaśyapo dhruvaḥ  BndP tārakāḥ śiśumārasya nāstaṃ yāti catuṣṭayam nakṣatracandramūryāśca grahāstārāgaṇaiḥ saha  BndP unmukhā vimukhāḥ sarve vakrībhūtāḥ śritā divi śānaiscaraṃ tathā baudhaṃ budho tha svarbhānuḥ svarbhānusthānamāsthitaḥ  BndP nakṣatrāṇi ca sarvāṇi nakṣatrāṇi viśantyuta gṛhāṇyetāni sarvāṇi jyotīṃṣi sukṛtātma nām  BndP kalpādau saṃpravṛttāni tapodhanāḥ  BndP yattadagre samutpannaṃ mathyamāne mahodadhau viṣaṃ kālānalaprakhyaṃ kālakūṭamiti śrutam  BndP yena prodbhūtamātreṇa na vyarājanta devatāḥ tasya viṣṇurahaṃ vāpi sarve vā surapuṅgavāḥ  BndP na śaknuvanti vai soḍhuṃ vegamanyatra śaṅkarāt ityuktvā padmagarbhābhaḥ padmāyonirayonijaḥ  BndP oṅkāraṃ samanusmṛtya dhyāyañjayotiḥ samantataḥ tataḥ stotuṃ samārabdho brahmā veda vidāṃ varaḥ  BndP namastubhyaṃ virūpākṣa namaste divyacakṣuṣe namaḥ pinākahastāya vajrahastāya vai namaḥ  BndP namastrailokya nāthāya bhūtānāṃ pataye namaḥ namaḥ surārihantre ca somasūryāgnicakṣuṣe  BndP brahmaṇe caiva rudrāya viṣṇave caiva te namaḥ sāṃkhyāya caiva yogāya bhūtagrāmāya vai namaḥ  BndP manmathāṅgavināśāya kālapṛṣṭhāya vai namaḥ suretase tha rudrāya devadevāya raṃhase  BndP kapardine karālāya śaṅkarāya harāya ca kapāline virūpāya śivāya varadāya ca  BndP tripuraghnamakhaghnāya mātṝṇāṃ pataye namaḥ vṛddhāya caiva śuddhāya muktāyaiva balāya ca  BndP lokatrayaikavīrāya candrāya varuṇāya ca agrāya caiva cogrāya viprāyānekacakṣuṣe  BndP rajase caiva sattvāya namaste vyaktayonaye nityāya caivānityāya nityānityāya vai namaḥ  BndP vyaktāya caivāvyaktāya vyaktāvyaktāya vai namaḥ cintyāya caivācintyāya cintyācintyāya vai namaḥ  BndP jagatāmārttināśāya priyanārāyaṇāya ca umāpriyāya śarvāya nandivaktrāṅkitāya ca  BndP pakṣamāsāhddhamāsāya ṛtusaṃvatsarāya ca bahurūpāya muṇḍāya daṇḍine ca varūthine  BndP namaḥ kapālahastāya digvāsāya śikhaṇḍine dhanvine rathine caiva yamine brahmacāriṇe  BndP ṛgyajuḥ sāmavedāya puruṣāyeśvarāya ca ityeva mādicaritaiḥ stotraiḥ stutya namīstu te evaṃ stutvā tato brahmā praṇipatya varānane  BndP jñātvā tu bhaktiṃ mama devatānāṃ gaṅgājalā sphālitamuktakeśaḥ sūkṣmo si yogātiśayādacintyo na hi prabho vyaktimuphaiṣi rudraḥ  BndP evaṃ bhagavatā pūrvaṃ brahmaṇā lokakartṛṇā stuto haṃ vividhaiḥ stotrairvedavedāṅgasaṃbhavaiḥ  BndP tato haṃ mukhyayā vācā pitāmahamathābravam bhūtabhavyabhavannātha lokanātha jagatpate  BndP kiṃ kāryaṃ te mayā brahmankarttavyaṃ vada suvrata śrutvā vākyaṃ tato brahmā pratyuvācāṃbujekṣaṇaḥ  BndP bhūtabhavyabhavannātha śrūyatāṃ kāraṇeśvara surāsurairmathyamāne payodhau paṅkajekṣaṇa  BndP bhagavanmeghasaṃkāśaṃ nīlajīmūtasannibham prādurbhūtaṃ viṣaṃ ghoraṃ saṃvarttāgnisamaprabham  BndP taṃ dṛṣṭvā ca vayaṃ sarve bhītāḥ saṃbhrāntacetasaḥ tatpibasva mahādeva lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā  BndP bhavāñchaktaśca bhoktā vai paraṃ vismayamājagāma  BndP tataḥ muragaṇāḥ sarve sadaityoragarākṣasāḥ ūcuḥ prāñjalayo bhūtvā mattamātaṅgagāmini  BndP ahobalaṃ vīryaparākramaste tvaho vapuryogabalaṃ taveśa  BndP aho prabhutvaṃ tava śubhām tasyāhaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi phalaṃ suvipulaṃ mahat  BndP viṣaṃ tasya varārohe sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ tathā gātraṃ prāpya tu suśroṇi kṣapraṃ tatpratihanyate  BndP śamāyatyaśubhaṃ ghoraṃ duḥkhapnaṃ paṭhecca devi bhaktyā ca pāṭhayecca naraḥ sadā  BndP ataḥ parataraṃ stotraṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati nāpi yakṣāḥ piśācā vā na bhūtā na vināyakāḥ kuryurvighnaṃ gṛhe tasya yatrāyaṃ tiṣṭhati stavaḥ  BndP mayā nu tuṣṭena tavāṃbujekṣaṇe stavasya māhātmyama ghaughanāśanam niveditaṃ puṇyaphalādiyuktaṃ svayaṃ ca kītaṃ caturānanena  BndP kathāmimāṃ puṇyaphalādiyuktāṃ nivedya devyai śaśibaddhamūrddhajaḥ mahādevasya māhātmyaṃ śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ ca naḥ  BndP kathaṃ dāruvaṇe devaṛṣisaṃghaniṣevite cakāra veṣaṃ vikṛtaṃ yena buddhā maharṣayaḥ  BndP jñātvā ca te mahādevaṃ tato bhrāntā hyacetasaḥ ārādhayanprasādārthaṃ naiṣāṃ tuṣṭaḥ punarbhavaḥ  BndP etatsarvaṃ yathāvṛttaṃ devadevena ceṣṭitam tatsarvaṃ kathayasveha tvaṃ no buddhimatāṃ varaḥ  BndP sūta uvācaśrūyatāmabhidhāsyāmi dharmametamatandritāḥ nirmmitaṃ devadevena bhaktānāmanukaṃpayā  BndP purā kṛtayuge viprāḥ śṛṅge himavataḥ śubhe devadāruvanaṃ ramyaṃ nānādrumalatākulam  BndP bahavo munayastatra tapasyanto munivratāḥ śaivāla bhojanāḥ kecitkecidantarjaleśayāḥ  BndP kecidabhrāvakāśāstu pādāṅguṣṭhāgradhiṣṭhitāḥ dantolūkhalinaścānye tvaśmakuṭṭāstathā pare  BndP sthānavīrāsanāścānye mṛgayaryāratāstathā kālaṃ nayanti tapasā tīvreṇa ca mahādhiyaḥ  BndP tatasteṣāṃ prasādārtha devastadvanamāgataḥ bhasmapāṇḍuradigdhāṅgo nagno vikṛtalakṣaṇaḥ  BndP vikṛtasrastakeśaśca karāladaśanastathā ulmukavyagrahastaśca raktapiṅgalalocanaḥ  BndP śiśnaṃ savṛṣaṇaṃ tasya raktagairikasannibham mukhamaṅgāravarṇena śuklena ca vibhūṣitam  BndP kvacitsa hasate raudraṃ kvacidgāyati vismi taḥ kvacinnṛtyati śṛṅgārī kvacidrauti muhurmuhuḥ  BndP nṛtyanta rurudhustūrṇaṃ patnyasteṣāṃ vimohitāḥ āśrame bhyāgato bhīkṣṇaṃ yā cate ca punaḥ punaḥ  BndP bhāryā kṛtā tathārūpā tṛṇābharaṇabhūṣitā vṛṣanādaṃ pragarjanvai kharanādaṃ nanāda ca  BndP tathā vañcitumā rabdho hāsayansarvadehinaḥ tataste munayaḥ kruddhāḥ krodhena kaluṣīkṛtāḥ  BndP mohitā māyayā sarve śapituṃ samupasthitāḥ karavadgāyase yasmātkharastasmādbhaviṣyasi  BndP rākṣaso vā piśāco vā dānavo vātha vā tathā yathā vaicchaṃstathā sarve kruddhāste munayaḥ samam  BndP śepuḥ śāsaistu vividhaistaṃ devaṃ bhuvaneśvaram tapāṃsi teṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ pratyāhanyanta śaṅkare  BndP yathādityaprakāśena tārakā nabhasi sthitāḥ na dyotante prakāśena tadvattejāṃsi śaṅkare  BndP śrūyate ṛṣiśāpena brahmaṇaḥ sumahātmanaḥ samṛddhaḥ śreyasāṃ yauniryajño vai nāśamāptavān  BndP bhṛgorapi ca śāpena viṣṇuḥ paramaviyavān prādurbhāvāndaśa prāpto duḥkhitaśca sadā kṛtaḥ  BndP indrasyāpi hi dharmajñaḥ śiśnaṃ savṛṣaṇaṃ purā ṛṣiṇā gautamenorvyāṃ kruddhena vinipātitam  BndP garbhavāso vasūnāṃ ca śāpena vihita stathā ṛṣīṇāṃ caiva śāpena nahuṣaḥ sarpatāṃ gataḥ  BndP kṣīrodaśca samudraśca hyapeyo brāhmaṇaiḥ kṛtaḥ dharmaścātra praśapto vai māṇḍavyena mahātmanā  BndP ete cānye ca bahavo yātanāṃ ca brahmacarya ratānāṃ ca vane vā vanavāsinām  BndP yatīnāṃ vā tathā dharmo nāyaṃ dṛṣṭaḥ kathañcana anayastu mahāneṣa yenāyaṃ mohito dvijāḥ  BndP liṅgaṃ prapātayasvaitannāyaṃ dharmastapasvinām vadasva vācā madhuraṃ vastramekaṃ samāśraya  BndP tyājite ca tvayā liṅge tataḥ pūjāmavāpsyasi ṛṣīṇāṃ tadvacaḥ śrutvā bhagavānbhaganetrahā  BndP uvāca ślakṣṇayā vācā prahasanniva śaṅkaraḥ na śakyamidamasmā kaṃ pratdṛṣṭendriyaceṣṭitaḥ  BndP sarveṣāṃ paśyatāmeva tatraivāntardadhe prabhuḥ antarhite bhagavati tathā liṅge kṛte bhave  BndP trailokye sarvabhūtānāṃ prādurbhāvo na jāyate vyākulaṃ ca tadā sarvaṃ na dhyānādvijñāya ceśvaram  BndP pratyuvāca tato brahmā vākyaṃ ca susamā hitaḥ eṣa devo mahādevo vijñeyastu maheśvaraḥ  BndP na tasya paramaṃ kiñcitpadaṃ samadhigamyate devānāṃ ca ṛṣīṇāṃ ca pitṛṇāṃ caiva sa prabhuḥ  BndP sahasrayugaparyante pralaye sarvadehinām saṃharatyeṣa bhagavān kālo bhūtvā maheśvaraḥ  BndP eṣa caiva prajāḥ sarvāḥ sṛjatyekaḥ svatejasā eṣa cikrī ca vakṣojaśrīvatsakṛtalakṣaṇaḥ  BndP yegī kṛtayuge caiva tretāyāṃ kraturucyate dvāpare caiva kālāgnirdharmaketuḥ kalau smṛtaḥ  BndP rudrasya mūrttayastisro vijñeyāścāpi paṇḍitaiḥ tamo hyagnī rajo brahmā sattvaṃ viṣṇuḥ prakāśakaḥ  BndP mūrttirekā smṛtā yasya digvāsāśca śivāhvayā yatra tiṣṭhanti tadbrahmayogena tu samanvitam  BndP tasmāddevaṃ devadevamī śānaṃ prabhumavyayam ārādhayata viprendrā jitakrodhā jitendriyāḥ  BndP dṛṣṭaṃ vai kṛtvā brahmāṇamamitaujasam āsthitā vītaśokāste devadāruvane tataḥ  BndP ārādhayitumārabdhā brahmaṇā kathitaṃ yathā sthaṇḍileṣu vicitreṣu parvateṣu guhāsu ca  BndP nadīnāṃ ca vicitreṣu pulineṣu śubheṣu vāgbhirgirīśamidamabruvan ajñānāddevadevasya yadasmābhignuṣṭhitam  BndP karmaṇā manasā vācā tatsarvaṃ kṣantumarhasi caritāni vicitrāṇi guhyāni gahanāni ca  BndP brahmādīnāṃ ca devānāṃ durvijñeyāni śaṅkara svāgataṃ te na jānīmo gatiṃ naiva ca naiva ca  BndP viśveśvara mahādeva yo si so si namo stu te stuvanti tvāṃ mahātmāno devadevaṃ maheśvaram  BndP namo bhavāya bhavyāya bhāvanāyodbhavāya ca anantabalavīryāya bhūtānāṃ pataye namaḥ  BndP saṃhartre kapiśāṅgāya avyayāya vyayāya ca gaṅgā saliladhārāya cādhārāya guṇātmane  BndP tryaṃbakāya trinetrāya triśūlavaradhāriṇe kandarpāya namastubhyaṃ namo stu paramātmane  BndP śakarāya vṛṣāṅkāya gaṇānāṃ pataye namaḥ daṇḍahastāya kālāya pāśahastāya vai namaḥ  BndP vedamantrapradhānāya śatajihvāya te namaḥ bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyacca sthāvaraṃ garimā pañcamī caiva ṣaṣṭhaṃ prākāmyameva ca īśitvaṃ ca vaśitvaṃ ca hyamaratvaṃ ca te gatāḥ  BndP indrādayastathā devāḥ kāmikaṃ vratamāsthitāḥ aiśvaryaṃ paramaṃ prāpya sarve prathitatejasaḥ  BndP sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā rudralokaṃ sa gacchati  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte pūrvabhāge dvitīye nuṣaṅgapāda dāruvanapraveśabhasmasnānavidhirnāma saptaviṃśatitamo BndP sa gacchati tadā draṣṭuṃ divākaraniśākarau amāvasyāmamāvāsyāṃ mātāmahapitāmahau  BndP abhivādya sa tau tatra kālāpekṣaḥ pratīkṣate prasyandamānātsomāttu pitrarthaṃ tu pariśravān  BndP ailaḥ purūravā vidvānmāsaśrāddhacikīrṣayā upāste pitṛmantaṃ taṃ somaṃ divi samāsthitaḥ  BndP dvilavāṃ kuhūmātrāṃ ca te ubhe tu vicārya saḥ sinīvālīpramāṇebhyaḥ sinīvālīmupāsya saḥ  BndP kuhūmātraḥ kalāṃ caiva jñātvopāste kuhūṃ tathā sa tadā tāmupāsīnaḥ kālāpekṣaḥ prapaśyati  BndP sudhāmṛtaṃ tu tatsomātsravadvai māsatṛptaye daśabhiḥ pañcabhiścaiva sudhāmṛtaparisravaiḥ  BndP kṛṣṇapakṣe bhujāṃ prītyā dahyamānāṃ tathāṃśubhiḥ sadyaḥ prakṣaratā tena saumyena madhunā tu saḥ  BndP nirvāteṣtratha pakṣeṣu pitryeṇa vidhinā divi sudhāmṛtena rājaindrastarpa yāmāsa vai pitṝn  BndP saumyānbarhiṣadaḥ kāvyānagniṣvāttāṃstathaiva ca ṛtamagnistu yaḥ proktaḥ sa tu saṃvatsaro mataḥ  BndP jajñire hyṛtavastasmāddhyṛtubhyaścārttavāstathā ārtavā hyarddhamāsākhyāḥ pitaro hyṛtusūnavaḥ  BndP ṛtavaḥ pitāmahā māsā ayanāhyabdasūnavaḥ prapitāmahāstu vai devāḥ pañcābdā brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ  BndP saumyāstu somajā jñeyāḥ kāvyā jñeyāḥ kaveḥ sutāḥ upahūtāḥ smṛtā devāḥ somajāḥ somapāḥ smṛtāḥ  BndP ājyapāstu smṛtāḥ kāvyāstisrastāḥ pitṛjātayaḥ kāvyā barhiṣada ścaiva agniṣvāttāśca tāstridhā  BndP gṛhasthā ye ca yajvāna ṛturbarhiṣado dhruvam gṛhasthāścāpyayajvāna agniṣvāttāstathārttavāḥ  BndP aṣṭakāpatayaḥ kāvyāḥ divākīrtyāśca te smṛtāḥ ye te pibantyamāvasyāṃ māsimāsi sudhāṃ divi  BndP tāṃstena tarpayāmāsa yāvadāsītpurūravāḥ yasmātprasravate somānmāsi māsi dhinoti ca  BndP tasmātsudhāmṛtaṃ tadvai pitṝṇāṃ somapāyinām evaṃ tadamṛtaṃ saumyaṃ sudhā ca madu caiva ha  BndP kṛṣṇapakṣe yathā vendoḥ kalāḥ pañcadaśa kramāt pibantyaṃbumayaṃ devāstrayastriṃśattu chandanāḥ  BndP pītvārddhamāsaṃ gacchanti caturdaśyāṃ sudhāmṛtam ityevaṃ pīyamānaistu devaiḥ sarvairniśākaraḥ  BndP samāgacchatyamāvasyāṃ bhāge pañcadaśe sthitaḥ suṣumṇāpyāyitaṃ caiva hyamāvasyāṃ yathā kramam  BndP pibanti dvilavaṃ kālaṃ pitaraste sudhāmṛtam pītakṣayaṃ tataḥ somaṃ sūryo sāvekaraśminā  BndP āpyāyayatsuṣumṇātaḥ punastānsomapāyinaḥ niḥ śeṣāyāṃ kalāyāṃ tu somamāpyāyayatpunaḥ  BndP suṣumṇāpyāyamānasya bhāgaṃ bhāgamahaḥ śuklakṛṣṇayoḥ ityevaṃ pitṛmānsomaḥ smṛta iḍvatsarātmakaḥ  BndP krāntaḥ pañcadaśaiḥ sārddhaṃ sudhāmṛtaparisravaiḥ ataḥ parvāṇi vakṣyāmi varvaṇāṃ saṃdhayaśca ye  BndP granthimanti yathā parvāṇīkṣuve kāvyāśca ayajvāno hyaconijāḥ devāste pitaraḥ sarve devāstānvādayantyuta  BndP manuṣyapitaraścaiva tebhyo nye laukikāḥ smṛtāḥ pitā pitāmahaścāpi tathā yaḥ prapitāmahaḥ  BndP yajvāno ye tu sāmena niyutānyeva ṣaḍiṃśānnirasāni yugāni vai  BndP catvāriṃśattathā trīṇi niyutā nīha saṃkhyayā viṃśatiśca sahasrāṇi sa saṃdhyāṃśaścaturyugaḥ  BndP evaṃ caturyugākhyānāṃ sādhikā hyekasaptatiḥ kṛtatretādiyuktānāṃ manorantaramucyate  BndP manvantarasya saṃkhyāṃ tu varṣāgreṇa nibodhata triṃśatkoṭyastu varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣeṇa prakīrttitāḥ  BndP sapta ṣaṣṭistathānyāni niyutānyadhikāni tu viśatiśca sahasrāṇi kālo yaṃ sādhikaṃ vinā  BndP manvantarasya saṃkhyaiṣā saṃkhyā vidbhirdvijaiḥ smṛtā manvantarasya kālo yaṃ yugaiḥ sārddhaṃ ca kīrttitaḥ  BndP catuḥ sāhasrayuktaṃ vai prākṛtaṃ tatkṛtaṃ yugam tretāśiṣṭaṃ pravakṣyāmi dvāparaṃ kalimeva ca  BndP yugapatsamayenārtho dvidhā vaktuṃ na śakyate kramāgataṃ mayā hyetattubhyaṃ nokta yuga dvayam  BndP ṛṣivaṃśaprasaṃgena vyākulatvāttathaiva ca atra tretāyugasyādau manuḥ saptarṣayaśca ye  BndP śrauta smārtta ca te dharma brahmaṇānupracauditam dārāgnihotrasaṃbandhamṛgyajuḥ sāmasaṃhitam  BndP ityādilakṣaṇaṃ śrautaṃ dharma saptarṣayo bruvan paraṃparāgataṃ dharma smārttaṃ cācāralakṣaṇam  BndP varṇāśramācārayutaṃ manuḥ svāyaṃbhuvo bravīt satyena brahmacaryeṇa śrutena tapasā ca vai  BndP teṣāṃ tu taptatapasā ārṣeṇopakrameṇa tu saptarṣīṇāṃ manoścaiva hyādye tretāyuge tathā  BndP abuddhipūrvakaṃ teṣāmakriyāpūrvameva ca abhivyaktāstu te mantrāstārakādyairnidarśanaiḥ  BndP ādikalpe tu devānāṃ prādurbhūtāstu yāḥ svayam prāṇāśeṣvatha siddhīnāmanyāsāṃ ca pravarttanam  BndP āsanmantrā vyatīteṣu ye kalpeṣu sahasraśaḥ te mantrā vai punasteṣāṃ pratibhāyāmupasthitāḥ  BndP ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāni mantraścātharvaṇāni tu saptarṣibhistu te proktāḥ smārttaṃ dharmaṃ manurjagau  BndP tretādau saṃhitā vedāḥ kevalā dharmasetavaḥ saṃrodhādāyuṣaścaiva vartsyante dvāpareṣu vai  BndP ṛṣayastapasā vedāndvāparādiṣvadhīyate anādinidhinā divyāḥ pūrvaṃ sṛṣṭāḥ svayaṃbhuvā  BndP sadharmāḥ savratāḥ sāṃgā yathādharmaṃ yugeyuge vikriyante samānārthā vedavādā yathāyugam  BndP āraṃbhayajñāḥ kṣatrāśca haviryajñā viśastathā paricārayajñāḥ śūdrāstu japayajñā dvijottamāḥ  BndP tadā pramuditā varṇāstretāyāṃ dharmapālitāḥ kriyāvantaḥ prajāvantaḥ samṛddhāḥ sukhinastathā  BndP brāhmaṇānanurttante kṣatriyāḥ kṣatriyānviśaḥ vaiśyānuvarttinaḥ śudrāḥ parasparamanuvratāḥ  BndP śubhāḥ pravṛttayasteṣāṃ dharmā varṇāśramāstathā saṃkalpitena manasā vācoktena svakarmaṇā  BndP tretāyuge ca viphalaḥ karmāraṃbhaḥ prasiddhyati āyurmedhā balaṃ rūpamārogyaṃ dharmaśīlatā  BndP sarvasādhāraṇā hyete tretāyāṃ vai bhavaṃ tyuta varṇāśramavyavasthānaṃ teṣāṃ brahmā tadākarot  BndP punaḥ prajāstu tā mohāddharmā stānapyapālayan parasparavirodhena manuṃ tāḥ punarabhyayuḥ  BndP punaḥ svāyaṃbhuvo dṛṣṭvā yāthātathyaṃ prajāpatiḥ dhyātvā tu śatarūpāyāṃ putrau sa udapādayat  BndP priyavrato ttānapādau prathamau tau mohīkṣitau tataḥ prabhṛti rājāna utpannā daṇḍadhāriṇaḥ  BndP prajānāṃ rañjanāccaiva rājānaste bhavannṛpāḥ pracchanna pāpāstairye ca na śakyāstu narādhipaiḥ  BndP dharmarājaḥ smṛtasteṣāṃ śāstā vaivasvato yamaḥ varṇānāṃ pravibhāgāśca tretāyāṃ saṃprakīrttitāḥ  BndP saṃbhṛtācca tadā mantrā ṛṣibhirbrahmaṇaḥ sutaiḥ yajñāḥ pravarttitāścaiva tadā hyeva tu daivataiḥ  BndP yāmaśukrārjitaiścaiva sarvasādhana saṃbhṛtaiḥ sārddhaṃ viśvabhujā caiva devendreṇa mahaujasā  BndP svāyaṃbhuveṃtare devairyajñastaiḥ prākpravarttitaḥ satyaṃ japastapo dānaṃ tretāyā dharma ucyate  BndP tadā dharmmasahasrānte hiṃsādharmaḥ pravarttate jāyante ca tadā śūrā āyuṣmanto mahābalāḥ  BndP vyastadaṇḍā mahābhāgā dharmiṣṭhā brahmavādinaḥ padmapatrāyatākṣāśca pṛthūraskāḥ susaṃhatāḥ  BndP siṃhātaṅkā mahāsattvā mattamātaṅgagaminaḥ mahādhanurddharāścaiva tretāyāṃ cakravarttinaḥ  BndP sarvalakṣaṇasampūrmā nyagrodhaparimaṇḍalāḥ nyagrodhau tu smṛtau bāhū vyāmo nyagrodha ucyate  BndP vyāme naivochrayo yasya sama ūrddhaṃ tu dehinaḥ samochrayaparīṇāho jñeyo nyagrodhamaṇḍalaḥ  BndP cakraṃ ratho maṇirbhāryā nidhiraśvo gajastathā saptaitāni ca ratnāni sarveṣāṃ cakravartināma  BndP cakraṃ ratho maṇiḥ khaḍgaścarmaratnaṃ ca pañcamam keturnidhiśca saptaiva prāṇahīnāni cakṣate  BndP bhāryā purohitaścaiva senānī rathakṛcca yaḥ mantryaśvaḥ kalabhaścaiva prāṇinaḥ sapta kīrttitāḥ  BndP ratnānyetāni divyāni saṃsiddhāni mahātmanām caturdaśa vidheyāni sarveṣāṃ cakravarttinām  BndP viṣṇoraṃśena jāyante pṛthivyāṃ cakravarttinaḥ manvantareṣu sarveṣu atītānāgateṣviha  BndP bhūtabhavyāni yānīha varttamānāni yāni ca tretāyuge ca tānyatra jāyante cakravarttinaḥ  BndP bhadrāṇīmāni teṣāṃ vai bhavantīha mahīkṣitām atyadbhutāni catvāri balaṃ dharmaḥ sukhaṃ dhanam  BndP anyonyasyāvirodhena prāpyante tu nṛpaiḥ samam artho dharmaśca kāmaśca yaśo vijaya eva ca  BndP aiśvaryeṇāṇimādyena prabhuśaktyā tathaiva ca śrutena tapasā caiva munīnabhibhavanti vai  BndP balena tapasā caiva devadānavamānavān lakṣaṇaiścaiva jāyante śarīrasthairamānuṣaiḥ  BndP keśāḥsnigdhā lalāṭoccā jihvā cāsya pramārjinī tāmraprabhoṣṭanetrāśca śrīvatsāścaiddhvaromaśāḥ  BndP ājānubāhavaschaiva tadāmrahastāḥ kaṭau kṛśāḥ nyagrodhapariṇāhāśca siṃhaskandhāstu mehanāḥ  BndP gajedragatayaścaiva mahāhanava eva ca pādayoścakramatsyontu śaṅkhapadmau tuhastayoḥ  BndP pañcāśītisahasrāṇi te rājantyajarā nṛpāḥ asaṃgagatayasteṣāṃ catasraścakravarttinām  BndP antarikṣe samudri ca pātāle parvateṣu ca ijyā dānaṃ tapaḥ satyaṃ tretāyāṃ dharma ucyate  BndP tadā pravarttate dharmo varṇāśramavibhāgaśaḥ maryādāsthāpanārthaṃ ca daṇḍanītiḥ pravarttate  BndP tdṛṣṭapuṣṭāḥ prajāḥ sarvā arogāḥ pūrṇamānasāḥ eko vedaścatuṣpādastretāyugavidhausmṛtaḥ  BndP trīṇi varṣasahasrāṇi tadā jīvanti mānavāḥ putrapautrasamākīrṇā mriyante ca krameṇa tu  BndP eṣa tretāyuge dharmastretāsaṃdhyāṃ nibodhata tretāyugasvabhāvānāṃ saṃdhyā pādena varttate saṃdhyāpādaḥ svabhāvastu soṃśapadena tiṣṭhati  BndP iti śrī brahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte pūrvabhāge dvitīye nuṣaṅgapāde saṃkhyāvartto nāmaikonatriśattamo dhyāyaḥśāṃśāpāyaniruvācakathaṃ tretāyugamukhe yajñasya syātpravarttanam pūrvaṃ svāyaṃbhuve sarge yathāvattacca brūhi me  BndP antarhitāyāṃ saṃdhyāyāṃ sārddhaṃ kṛtayugena vai kālākhyāyāṃ pravṛttāyāṃ prāpte tretāyuge tadā  BndP auṣadhīṣu ca jātāsu pravṛtte vṛṣṭisarjane pratiṣṭhitāyāṃ vārttāyāṃ gṛhāśramapare punaḥ  BndP varṇāśramavyavasthānaṃ kṛtavantaśca saṃkhyayā saṃbhārāṃstāṃstu maṃbhṛtya kathaṃ yajñaḥ pravarttitaḥ  BndP etacchutvābravītsūtaḥ śrūyatāṃ śāṃśapāyane yathā tretāyugamukhe yajñasya syātpravartanam  BndP pūrvaṃ svāyaṃbhuve sarge tadvakṣyāmyānupūrvyataḥ antarhitāyāṃ saṃdhyāyāṃ sārddhaṃ kṛtayugena tu  BndP kālākhyāyāṃ pravṛttāyāṃ prapte tretāyuge tadā auṣadhīṣu ca jātāsu pravṛtte vṛṣṭisarjane  BndP pratiṣṭhitāyāṃ vārttāyāṃ gṛhaśramapareṣu ca varṇāśramavyavasthānaṃ kṛtvā mantrāṃstu saṃhatān  BndP mantrāṃstānyojayitvātha ihāmutra ca karmasu tadā viśvabhugindraśca yajñaṃ prāvarttayatprabhuḥ  BndP daivataiḥ sahitaiḥ sarvaiḥ sarvasaṃbhārasaṃbhṛtaiḥ tasyāśvamedhe vitate samājagmurmaharṣayaḥ  BndP yajantaṃ paśubhirme dhyairūcuḥ sarve samāgatāḥ karmavyagreṣu ṛtvikṣu saṃtate yajñakarmaṇi  BndP saṃpragītheṣu sarveṣu sāmageṣvatha susvagm parikrānteṣu laghuṣu hyadhvaryuvṛṣabheṣu ca  BndP ālabdheṣu ca medhyeṣu tathā paśugaṇeṣu ca haviṣyagnau hūyamāne brāhmaṇaiścāgnihotribhiḥ  BndP āhūteṣu ca sarveṣu yajñabhākṣu prapacchuridraṃ saṃbhūya ko yaṃ yajña vidhistava  BndP adharmo balavāneṣa hiṃsādharmepsayā tataḥ tataḥ paśuvadhaścaiṣa tava yajñe surottama  BndP adharmo dharmaghātāya prārabdhaḥ paśuhisayā nāyaṃ dharmo hyadharmo yaṃ na hiṃsā dharma ucyate  BndP āgamena bhavānyajñaṃ karotu yadihecchati vidhidṛṣṭena yajñena dharmeṇāvyapasetunā  BndP yajñabīcaiḥ sureśraṣṭha yeṣu hiṃsā na vidyate trivarṣaṃ yaṣṭavyamiti cocyate  BndP te tu khinnā vivādena tattvamuttvā maharṣayaḥ sandhāya vākyamindreṇa papracchuḥ khecaraṃ vasum  BndP sahāprājña kathaṃ dṛṣṭastvayā yajñavidhirnṛpa auttānapāde prabrūhi bījaiḥ phalairapi  BndP hiṃsāsvabhāvo yajñasya iti me darśanāgamau yatheha devatā mantrā hiṃsāliṅgā maharṣibhiḥ  BndP dīrgheṇa tapasā yuktairdarśanaistārakādibhiḥ tatprāmāṇyānmayā coktaṃ tasmātsa prāptumarhatha  BndP yadi pramāṇaṃ tānyeva mantravākyāni vai dvijāḥ tathā pravatatāṃ yajño hyanyathā vo nṛtaṃ vacaḥ  BndP evaṃ kṛtottarāste vai yuktātmānastapodhanāḥ avaśyabhāvitaṃ dṛṣṭvā tamatho vāgyatābhavan  BndP ityuktamātre nṛpatiḥ praviveśa rasātalam ūrdhvacārī vasurbhūtvā rasātalacaro bhavat  BndP vasudhā talavāsī tu tena vākyena so bhavat dharmāṇāṃ saṃśayacchettā rājā vasuradhogataḥ  BndP tasmānna vācyamekena bahujñenāpi saṃśaye bahudvārasya dharmasya sūkṣmā dūratarā gatiḥ  BndP tasmānna niścayādvaktuṃ dharmaḥ śakyastu kenacit devānṛṣīnupādāya svāyaṃbhuvamṛte manum  BndP tasmādahiṃsā dharmasya dvāramuktaṃ maharṣibhiḥ ṛṣikoṭisahasrāṇi svatapobhirdivaṃ yayuḥ  BndP tasmānna dānaṃ yajñaṃ vā praśaṃsaṃti maharṣayaḥ uñchamūlaphalaṃ śākamudapātraṃ tapodhanāḥ  BndP etaddatvā vibhavataḥ svarge loke pratiṣṭhitāḥ adrohaścāpya lobhaśca tapo bhutadayā damaḥ  BndP brahmacaryaṃ tathā satyamanukrośaḥ kṣamā dhṛtiḥ sanātanasya dharmasya mūlametaddurāsadam  BndP śrūyante hi tapaḥsiddhā brahmakṣatrādayo naghāḥ priyavratottānapādau dhruvo medhātithirvasuḥ  BndP sudhāmā virajāścaiva śaṅkhaḥ pāṇḍyaja eva ca prājīnabarhiḥ parjanyo havirdhānādayo nṛpaḥ  BndP ete cānye ca bahavaḥ svaistapobhirdivaṃ gatāḥ rājarṣayo mahāsattvā yeṣāṃ kīrttiḥ pratiṣṭhitā  BndP tasmādviśiṣyate yajñāttapaḥ sarvaistu kāraṇaḥ brahmaṇā tapasā sṛṣṭaṃ jagadviśvamidaṃ purā  BndP tasmānnānveti tadyajñastapomūlamidaṃ smṛtam dravyamantrātmako yajñastapastvanaśanātmakam  BndP yajñena devānāpnoti vairājaṃ tapasā punaḥ brāhmaṃ tu karma saṃnyāsādvairāgyātprakṛterjayam  BndP jñānātprāpnoti kaivalyaṃ pañcaitāgatayaḥ smṛtāḥ evaṃ vivādaḥ sumahānya jñasyāsītpravarttane  BndP devatānāmṛṣīṇāṃ ca pūrva svāyaṃbhuve ntare tatastamṛṣayo dṛṣṭvā hataṃ dharmabalena tu  BndP vasorvākyamanā dṛtya jagamuḥ sarve yathāgatam gateṣu munisaṃgheṣu devā yajñaṃ samāpnuvan  BndP yajñapravarttanaṃ hyevamāsītsvāyaṃbhuve ntare tataḥ prabhṛti yajño yaṃ yugaiḥ saha vivarttitaḥ  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte pūrvabhāge dvitīye nuṣaṅgapāde yajñapravarttanaṃ nāma triśattamo dhyāyaḥsūta uvācaata ūrddhaṃ pravakṣyāmi dvāparasya vidhiṃ punaḥ tatra tretāyuge kṣīṇe dvāparaṃ pratipadyate  BndP dvāparādau prajānāṃ tu siddhistretāyuge tu yā parivṛtte yuge tasmiṃstatastābhiḥ praṇaśyati  BndP tataḥ pravarttate tāsāṃ prajānāṃ dvāpare punaḥ saṃbhedaścaiva varṇānāṃ kāryāṇāṃ ca viparyayaḥ  BndP yajñāvadhāraṇaṃ daṇḍo mado daṃbhaḥ kṣamā balam eṣā rajastamoyuktā pravṛttirdvāpare smṛtā  BndP ādye kṛte yo dharmo sti sa tretāyāṃ pravarttate dvāpare vyākulībhūtvā praṇaśyati kalau yuge  BndP varṇānāṃ viparidhvaṃsaḥ saṃkīyata tathāśramāḥ dvaividhyaṃ pratipadyeteyuge tasmiñchruti smṛtī  BndP dvaidhāttathā śrutismṛtyorniścayo nādhigamyate aniścayādhigamanāddharmatattvaṃ na vidyate  BndP dharmāsattvena mitrāṇāṃ matibhedo bhavennṛṇām parasparavibhinnaistaidṛṣṭīnāṃ vibhrameṇa ca  BndP ayaṃ dharmo hyayaṃ neti niścayo nādhigamyate kāraṇānāṃ ca vaikalpyātkāryāṇāṃ cāpyaniścayāt  BndP matibhedena teṣāṃ vai dṛṣṭīnāṃ vibhramo bhavet tato dṛṣṭivibhannaistu kṛtaṃ śāstrākulaṃ tvidam  BndP eko vedaścatuṣpāddhi tretāsviha vidhīyate saṃkṣayādāyupaścaiva vyasyate dvāpareṣu ca  BndP ṛṣimantrātpunarbhedādbhidyate dṛṣṭivibhramaiḥ mantrabrāhmaṇavinyāsaiḥ svaravarṇaviparyayaiḥ  BndP saṃhitā ṛgyajuḥsāmnāṃ saṃpaṭhyante maharṣibhiḥ sāmānyā vaikṛtāścaiva dṛṣṭibhinne kvacitkvacit  BndP brāhmaṇaṃ kalpasūtrāṇi mantrapravacanāni ca anye pi prasthitāstānvai kecittānpratyavasthitāḥ  BndP dvāpareṣu pravarttante nivarttante kalau yuge ekamādhvaryavaṃ tvāsītpunardvaidhamajāyata  BndP sāmānyaviparītārthaiḥ kṛtaśāstrākulaṃ tvidam ādhvaryavasya prasthānairbahudhā vyākulīkṛtaiḥ  BndP tathaivātharvaṛksāmnāṃ vikalpaiścāpi saṃjñayā vyākuledvāpare nityaṃ kriyate bhinna darśanaiḥ  BndP teṣāṃ bhedāḥ pratībhedā vikalpāścāpi saṃkhyāyā dvāpare saṃpravarttate vinaśyanti tataḥ kalau  BndP teṣāṃ viparyayotpannā bhavanti dvāpare punaḥ avṛṣṭirmaraṇaṃ caiva tathaiva vyādhyupadravāḥ  BndP vāṅmanaḥ karmarjeduḥkhairnirvedo jāyate punaḥ nirvedājjāyate teṣāṃ duḥkhamokṣavicāraṇā  BndP vicāraṇācca vairāgyaṃ vairāgyāddoṣadarśanam doṣadarśanatascaiva dvāpare jñānasaṃbhavaḥ  BndP teṣāma jñānināṃ pūrvamādye svāyaṃbhuve ntare utpadyante hi śāstrāṇāṃ dvāpare paripanthinaḥ  BndP āyurvedavikalpaśca hyagānāṃ jyotiṣasya ca arthaśāstravikalpāśca hetuśāstravikalpanam  BndP prakriyākalpasūtrāṇāṃ bhāṣyavidyāvikalpanam smṛtiśāstraprabhedaśca prasthānāni pṛthakpṛthak  BndP dvāpareṣvabhivarttante matibhedāśrayānnṛṇām manasā karmaṇā vācā kṛcchrādvārtā prasiddhyati  BndP dvāpare sarvabhūtānāṃ kāyakleśapuraskṛtā lobho vṛttirvaṇikpūrvā tattvānāmaviniścayaḥ  BndP vedaśāstrapraṇayanaṃ dharmāṇāṃ saṃkarastathā varṇāśramaparidhvaṃsaḥ kāmakrodhau tathaiva ca  BndP dvāpareṣu pravarttante rāgo lobho vadhastathā vedaṃ vyāsaścaturddhā tu vyasyate dvāparādiṣu  BndP niḥśeṣe dvāpare tasmiṃstasya saṃdhyā tu yādṛśī pratiṣṭhate guṇairhīno dharmo sau dvāparasya tu  BndP tathaiva saṃdhyā pādena hyaṅgaḥ saṃdhyā itīṣyate dvāparasyāvaśeṣeṇa tiṣyasya tu nibodhata  BndP dvāparasyāśaseṣaṇa pratipattiḥ kalerapi hiṃsāsūyānṛtaṃ māyā vadhaścaiva tapasvinām  BndP ete svabhāvāstiṣyasya sādhayanti ca vai prajāḥ eṣa dharmaḥ kṛtaḥ kṛtsno dharmaśca parihīyate  BndP manasā karmaṇā stutyā vārtā sidhyati vā na vā kalau pramārakī rogaḥ satataṃ kṣudbhayāni ca  BndP anāvṛṣṭibhayaṃ ghoraṃ deśānāṃ ca viparyayaḥ na pramāṇaṃ smṛterasti tiṣye lokeṣu vai yuge  BndP garbhastho mriyate kaścidyauva nasthastathāparaḥ sthavirāḥ ke pi kaumāre mriyante vai kalau prajāḥ  BndP duriṣṭairduradhītaiśca duṣkṛtaiśca durāgamaiḥ viprāṇāṃ karmadoṣaistaiḥ prajānāṃ jāyate bhayam  BndP hiṃsā māyā tatherṣyā ca krodho sūyā kṣamā nṛṣu tiṣye bhavanti jantūnāṃ rāgo lobhaśca sarvaśaḥ  BndP saṃkṣobho jāyate tyathai karimāsādya vai yugam pūrṇe varṣasahasre vai paramāyustadā nṛṇām  BndP nādhīyate tadā vedānna yajaṃ te dvijātayaḥ utsīdanti narāścaiva kṣatriyāśca viśaḥ kramāt  BndP śūdrāṇāmantyayonestu saṃbandhā brāhmaṇaiḥ saha bhavantīha kalau tasmiñchayanāsanabhojanaiḥ  BndP rājānaḥ śūdrabhūyiṣṭhāḥ pākhaṇḍānāṃ pravarttakāḥ guṇahīnāḥ prajāścaiva tadā vai saṃpravarttate  BndP āyurmedhā balaṃ rūpaṃ kulaṃ caiva praṇaśyati śūdrāśca brāhmaṇācārāḥ śūdrācārāśca brāhmaṇāḥ  BndP rājavṛttāḥ sthitāścorā ścorācārāśca pārthivāḥ bhṛtyā ete hyasubhṛto yugānte samavasthite  BndP aśīlinyo nṛtāścaiva striyo madyāmiṣapriyāḥ māyāvinyo bhaviṣyanti yugānte munisattama  BndP ekapatnyo na śiṣyanti yugānte munisattama śvāpadaprabalatvaṃ ca gavāṃ caiva hyupakṣayaḥ  BndP sādhūnāṃ vinivṛttiṃ ca vidyāstasminyugakṣaye tadā dharmo mahodarke durlabho dānamūlavān  BndP cāturāśramaśaithilyo dharmaḥ pravicariṣyati tadā hyalpaphalā bhūmiḥ kvaciccāpi mahāphalā  BndP na rakṣitāro boktāro balibhāgasya pārthivāḥ yugānte ca bhaviṣyanti svarakṣaṇaparāyaṇāḥ  BndP arakṣitāro rājāno viprāḥ śūdropajīvinaḥ śūdrābhivādinaḥ sarve yugānte dvijasattamāḥ  BndP adṛśūlā janapadāḥ śivaśūlā dvijāstathā pramadāḥ keśaśūlāśca yugānte samupasthite  BndP tapoyajñaphalānāṃ ca vikretāro dvijottamāḥ yatayaśca bhaviṣyanti bahavo sminkalau yuge  BndP citravarṣī yadā devastadā prāhuryugakṣayam sarve vāṇijakāścā pi bhaviṣyantyadhame yuge  BndP bhūyiṣṭhaṃ kūṭamānaiśca paṇyaṃ vikrīṇate janāḥ kuśīlacaryāpākhaṇḍairvyādharūpaiḥ samāvṛtam  BndP puruṣālpaṃ bahustrīkaṃ yugānte samupasthite bāhuyācanako loko bhaviṣyati parasparam  BndP avyākartā krūravākyā nārjavo nānasūyakaḥ na kṛte pratikarttā ca yuge kṣīṇe bhaviṣyati  BndP aśaṅkā caiva patite yugānte tasya lakṣaṇam tataḥ śūnya vasumatī bhaviṣyati vasundharā  BndP goptāraścāpyagoptāraḥ prabhaviṣyanti śāsakāḥ harttāraḥ pararatnānāṃ paradāravimarśakāḥ  BndP kāmātmāno durātmāno hyadhamāḥ sāhasapriyāḥ pranaṣṭaceṣṭanā dhūrttā muktakeśāsttvaśūlinaḥ  BndP ūnaṣoḍaśavarṣāśca prajā yante yugakṣaye śukladantā jitākṣāśca muṇḍāḥ kāṣāyavāsasaḥ  BndP śūdrā dharmaṃ cariṣyati yugānte samupasthite sasyacorā bhaviṣyanti tathā cailāpahāriṇaḥ  BndP corāccorāśca harttāro harturharttā tathāparaḥ jñānakarmamyuparate loke niṣkriyatāṃ gate  BndP kīṭamūṣakasarpāśca dharṣayiṣyanti mānavān abhīkṣṇaṃ kṣemamārogyaṃ sāmarthyaṃ durlabhaṃ tathā  BndP kauśikānprativatsyanti deśāḥ kṣudbhayapīḍitāḥ duḥkhenābhiplutānāṃ ca paramāyuḥ śataṃ tadā  BndP dṛśyante ca na dṛśyante vedā kaliyuge khilāḥ tatsīdante tathā yajñāḥ kevalādharmapīḍitāḥ  BndP kāṣāyiṇo tha nirgranthā tathā kāpālikāśca ha vedavikrayimaścanye tīrthavikrayiṇo pare  BndP varṇāśramāṇāṃ ye cānye pākhaṇḍāḥ paripanthinaḥ utpadyante tadā te vai saṃprāpte tu kalau yuge  BndP adhīyate tadā vedāñchūdrā dharmārtha kovidāḥ yajante cāśvamedhena rājānaḥ śūdrayonayaḥ  BndP strībālagovadhaṃ kṛtvā hatvānye ca parasparam apahatya tathānyonyaṃ sādhayanti tadā prajāḥ  BndP duḥkhapravacanālpāyurdehālpāyuśca rogataḥ adharmābhiniveśitvāttamovṛttaṃ kalau smṛtam  BndP prajāsu bhrūṇahatyā ca tadā vairātpravarttate tasmādāyurbalaṃ rūpaṃ kaliṃ prāpya prahīyate  BndP tadā cālpena kālena siddhiṃ gacchanti mānavāḥ dhanyā dharmaṃ cariṣyanti yugānte dvijasattamāḥ  BndP śrutismṛtyuditaṃ dharmaṃ ye carantyanasūyakāḥ tretāyāmābdiko dharmo dvāpare māsikaḥ smṛtaḥ  BndP yathāśakti caranprājñastadahnā prāpnuyātkalau eṣā kaliyugāvasthā saṃdhyāṃśaṃ tu nibodhata  BndP yugeyuge tu hīyante tritripādāstu siddhayaḥ yugasvabhāvātsaṃdhyāsu tiṣṭhantīha tu yādṛśaḥ  BndP saṃdhyāsvabhāvāḥ svāṃśeṣu pādaśeṣāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ evaṃ saṃdhyāṃśake kāle saṃprāpte tu yugāntike  BndP teṣāṃ śāstā hyasādhūnāṃ bhṛgūṇāṃ nidhanotthitaḥ gotreṇa vai candra maso nāmnā pramatirucyate  BndP mādhavasya tu soṃśena pūrvaṃ svāyaṃbhuve ntare samāḥ saviṃśatiḥ pūrṇāḥ paryaṭanvai vasuṃdharām  BndP anukarṣansa vai senāṃ savājirathakuñjarām pragṛhītāyudhairvipraiḥ śataśo tha sahasraśaḥ  BndP sa tadā taiḥ parivṛto mlecchānhanti smasarvaśaḥ saha vā sarvaśaścaiva rājñastāñchūdrayonijān  BndP pāravaṇḍāstu tataḥ sarvān niḥ śeṣaṃ kṛtavānvibhuḥ nātyartha dhārmikā ye ca tānsarvānhanti sarvaśaḥ  BndP varṇavyatyāsajātāśca ye ca tānanujīvinaḥ udīcyānmadhyadeśyāṃśca pavatīyāṃstathaiva ca  BndP prācyānpratīcyāṃśca tathā vindhyapṛṣṭhacarānapi tathaiva dākṣiṇātyāṃśca draviḍānsiṃhalaiḥ saha  BndP gāndhārānpāradāṃścaiva pahlavānyava nāñśakān tuṣārānbarbarāṃścīnāñchūlikāndaradān khaśān  BndP laṃpākārānsakatakānkirātānāṃ ca jātayaḥ pravṛttacakro balavānmlecchānāmantakṛtprabhuḥ  BndP adṛṣṭaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ cacārātha vasundharām mādhavasya tu soṃśena devasyeha vijajñivān  BndP pūrvajanmani vikhyātaḥ pramatirnnāma vīryavān gotrato vai candramasaḥ pūrve kaliyuge prabhuḥ  BndP dvātriṃśe bhyudite varṣe prakrānto viṃśatīḥ samāḥ vinighnansarvabhūtāni mānavāneva sarvaśaḥ  BndP kṛtvā bījāvaśeṣaṃ tu pṛthvyāṃ kūreṇa karmaṇā paraspara nimittena kopenākasmikena tu  BndP susādhayitvā vṛṣalānprāyaśastānadharmikān gaṅgāyamunayormadhye niṣṭhāṃ prāptaḥ sahānugaḥ  BndP tato vyatīte kalpe tu sāmānye sahasainikaḥ utsādya pārthivānsarvānmalecchāṃścaiva sahasraśaḥ  BndP tatra saṃdhyāṃśake kāle saṃprāpte tu yugāntake sthitāsvalpāvaśiṣṭāsu prajāsviha kvacitkvacit  BndP apagrahāstatastā vai lobhāviṣṭāstu vṛndaśaḥ upahisaṃti cānyonyaṃ pothayantaḥ parasparam  BndP arājake yugavaśātsaṃkṣaye samupasthite prajāstā vai tataḥ sarvāḥ parasparabhayārdditāḥ  BndP vyākulāśca paribhrāntāstyaktvā dārāngṛhāṇi ca svānpraṇānanapekṣanto niṣkāraṇasuduḥkhitāḥ  BndP naṣṭe śraute smṛtau dharme parasparahatāstadā nirmaryādā nirākrandā niḥsnehā nirapatrapāḥ  BndP naṣṭe dharme pratihatā hrasvakāḥ pañcaviṃśatim hitvā putrāṃśca dārāṃśca viṣādavyākuledriyāḥ  BndP anāvṛṣṭihatāścaiva vārttāmutsṛjya duḥkhitāḥ pratyantāṃstā niṣevante hitvā janapadānsvakān  BndP saritaḥ sāgarānūpānsevante parvatāṃstathā māṃsairmūlaphalaiścaiva vartayantaḥ suduḥkhitāḥ  BndP cīrapatrācinadharā niṣkriyā niṣparigrahāḥ varṇāśramaparibhraṣṭāḥ saṃkaraṃ ghoramāsthitāḥ etāṃ kāṣṭhāmanuprāptā alpaśeṣāḥ prajāstataḥ  BndP jarāvyādhikṣudhā viṣṭā duḥkhānnirvedamāgaman vicāraṇā tu nirvedātsāmyāvasthā vicāraṇāt  BndP sāmyāvasthātmako bodhaḥ saṃbodhāddharmaśīlatā tāsūpaśamayuktāsu kaliśiṣṭāsu vai svayam  BndP ahorātraṃ tadā tāsāṃ yugānte parivarttini cittasaṃmohanaṃ kṛtvā tāsāṃ vai suptamattavat  BndP bhāvinorthasya ca balāttataḥ kṛtamavarttata pravṛtte tu tatastasminpūte kṛtayuge tu vai  BndP utpannāḥ kaliśiṣṭāsu prajāḥ kārtayugāstadā tiṣṭhanti ceha ye siddhā adṛṣṭā vicaranti ca  BndP saha saptarṣibhiścaiva tatra te ca vyavasthitāḥ brahmakṣatraviśaḥ śūdrā bījārthaṃ ye smṛtā iha  BndP kalijaiḥ saha te saṃti nirviśeṣāstadābhavan teṣāṃ saptarṣayo dharmaṃ kathayantītareṣu ca  BndP varṇāśramācārayuktaḥ śrautaḥ smārtto dvidhā tu saḥ tatasteṣu kriyāvatsu vartante vai prajāḥ kṛte  BndP śrautasmārtte kṛtānāṃ ca dharme saptarṣidarśite keciddharmavyavasthārthaṃ tiṣṭhantīhāyugakṣayāt  BndP manvantarādhikāreṣu tiṣṭhanti munayastu vai yathā dāvapradagdheṣu tṛṇeṣviha tapena tu  BndP vanānāṃ prathamaṃ vṛṣṭyā teṣāṃ mūleṣu saṃbhavaḥ tathā kārtayugānāṃ tu kalijaṣviha saṃbhavaḥ  BndP evaṃ yugo yugasyeha saṃtānastu parasparam varttate hyavyavacchedādyāvanmanvantarakṣayaḥ  BndP sukhamāyurbalaṃ rūpandharmorthaḥ kāma eva ca yugeṣvetāni hīyante tritripādāḥ krameṇa ca  BndP sasaṃdhyāśeṣu hīyante yugānāndharmasiddhayaḥ ityeṣa pratisaṃdhiryaḥ kīrttitastu mayā dvijāḥ  BndP caturyugānāṃ sarveṣāmetenaiva prasādhanam eṣā caturyugāvṛttirāsahasradguṇīkṛtā  BndP brahmaṇastadahaḥ proktaṃ caturyuge yathaikasminbhavatīha yathā tu yat  BndP tathā cānyeṣu bhavati punastadvadyathākramam sarge sarge tathā bhedā utpadyante tathaiva tu  BndP pañcatriṃśatparimitā na nyūnā nādhikāḥ smṛtāḥ tathā parivarttamānaḥ  BndP ityeta llakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ yugānāṃ vai samāsataḥ  BndP atītānāgatānāṃ hi sarvamanvantaroṣviha manvantareṇa caikena sarvāṇyevāntarāṇi vai  BndP khyātānīha vijānīdhvaṃ kalpaṃ kalpena caiva ha anāgateṣu tadvacca tarkaḥ kāryo vijānatā  BndP manvantareṣu sarveṣu atītānāgateṣviha tulyābhimāninaḥ sarve nāmarūpairbhavantyuta  BndP devā hyaṣṭavidhā ye vā iha manvantareśvarāḥ ṛṣayo manavaścaiva sarve tulyāḥ prayojanaiḥ  BndP evaṃ varṇāśramāṇāṃ tu pravibhāgaṃ purā yuge yugasvabhāvāṃśca tathā vidhatte vai sadā prabhuḥ  BndP varṇāśramavibhāgāśca yugāni yugasiddhayaḥ anuṣaṅgātsamākhyātāḥ sṛṣṭisargaṃ nibodhata vistareṇānupūrvyā ca sthitiṃ vakṣye yugeṣviha  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte pūrvabhāge dvitīye nuṣaṅgapāde caturyugākhyānaṃ nāmaikatriṃśattamo dhyāyaḥsūta uvācayugeṣu yāstu jāyante prajāstā me nibodhata āsurī sarpagāndharvā paiśācī yakṣarākṣasī  BndP yasminyuge ca saṃbhūti stāsāṃ yāvacca jīvitam piśācāsuragandharvāṃ yakṣarākṣasapannagāḥ  BndP pariṇāhocchrayaistulyā jāyante ha kṛte yuge ṣaṇṇavatyaṅgulo tsedho hyaṣṭānāṃ devajanmanām  BndP svenāṅgulapramāṇena niṣpannena ca pauṣṭikāt etatsvābhāvikaṃ teṣāṃ pramāṇamiti kurvate  BndP manuṣyā āpādatalamastiṣko navatālo bhavettu yaḥ  BndP saṃhatā jānubāhustu sa surairapi pūjyate gavāśvahastināṃ caiva mahiṣa syāvarātmanām  BndP karmaṇaitena vijñeye hrāsavṛddhī yuge yuge mānuṣasya śarīrasya sanniveśastu yādṛśaḥ  BndP tallakṣaṇastu devānāṃ dṛśyeta tattvadarśanāt buddhyātiśayayuktaśca devānāṃ kāya ucyate  BndP tathā sātiśayaschaiva mānuṣaḥ kāya ucyate ityete vai sādhūṃstathaiva ca  BndP saditi brahmaṇaḥ śabdastadvanto ye bhavantyuta sājātyādbrahmaṇastvete tena santaḥ pracakṣate  BndP daśātmake ye viṣaye kāraṇe cāṣṭalakṣaṇe na krudhyanti na tdṛṣyanti yogasya sādhanāt  BndP evamāśramadharmāṇāṃ sādhanātsādhavaḥ smṛtāḥ gṛhastho brahmacārī ca vānaprastho yatistathā  BndP atha devā na pitaro munayo na ca mānuṣāḥ ayaṃ dharmo hyayaṃ neti vindate bhinnadarśanāḥ  BndP dharmādharmāvihaproktau śabdāvetau kriyātmakau kuśalākuśalaṃ karma dharmādharmāviha smṛtām  BndP dhāraṇartho dhṛtiścaiva dhātuḥ śabde prakīrttitaḥ adhāraṇāmahattve ca adharma iti svayamācarate yasmādācāraṃ sthāpayatyapi ācinoti ca śāstrāṇi ācāryastena cocyate  BndP dharmajñairvihito dharmaḥ śrautaḥ smārtto dvidhā dvijaiḥ dārāgnihotrasambandhāddvidhā śrautasya lakṣaṇam  BndP smārtto varṇāśramācārairyamaiḥ saniyamaiḥ smṛtaḥ pūrvebhyo vedayitveha śrautaṃ saptarṣa yo bruvan  BndP ṛco yajūṃsāmāni brahmaṇo ṅgāni ca śrutiḥ manvantarasyātītasya smṛtvācārānmanurjagau  BndP tasmā tsmārttaḥ dharmo varṇāśramavibhājakaḥ sa eṣa vividho dharmaḥ śiṣṭācāra ihocyate  BndP śeṣaśabdaḥ śiṣṭa iti śeṣaṃ śiṣṭaṃ pracakṣate manvantareṣu ye śiṣṭā iha tiṣṭhanti dhārmikāḥ  BndP manuḥ saptarṣayaścaiva lokasaṃtānakāramāt dharmārthaṃ ye ca tiṣṭhanti tāñchiṣṭānvai pracakṣate  BndP manvādayaśca ye śiṣṭā ye mayā prāgudīritāḥ taiḥ śiṣṭaiścarito dharmaḥ samyageva yuge yuge  BndP trayī vārttā daṇḍanītirijyā varṇāśramāstathā śiṣṭairācaryate yasmānmanunā ca punaḥ punaḥ  BndP pūrvaiḥ pūrvagatatvācca śiṣṭācāraḥ sa sātvataḥ dānaṃ satyaṃ tapo jñānaṃ vidyejyā vrajanaṃ dayā  BndP aṣṭau tāni caritrāṇi śiṣṭācārasya lakṣaṇam śiṣṭā yasmāccarantyenaṃ manuḥ saptarṣayastu vai  BndP manvantareṣu sarveṣu śiṣṭācārastataḥ smṛtaḥ vijñeyaḥ śravaṇācchrautaḥ smaraṇātsmārtta ucyate  BndP ijyāvedātmakaḥ śrautaḥ smārtto varṇāśramātmakaḥ pratyaṅgāni ca vakṣyāmi dharmasyeha tu lakṣaṇam  BndP dṛṣṭvā tu bhūtamarthaṃ yaḥ pṛṣṭo vai na nigū hati yathā bhūtapravādastu ityetatsatyalakṣaṇam  BndP brahmacaryaṃ japo maunaṃ nirāhāratvameva ca ityetattapaso rūpaṃ sughoraṃ sudurā sadam  BndP paśūnāṃ dravyahaviṣāmṛksāmayajuṣāṃ tathā ṛtvijāṃ dakṣiṇānāṃ ca saṃyogo yajña ucyate  BndP ātmavatsarvabhūteṣu yā hitāyāhitāya ca pravarttante samā dṛṣṭiḥ kṛtsnāpyeṣā dayā smṛtā  BndP ākruṣṭo nihato vāpi nākrośedyo na hanti ca vāṅmanaḥkarmabhirvetti titikṣaiṣā kṣamā smṛtā  BndP svāminā rakṣyamāṇānāmutsṛṣṭānāṃ ca saṃbhrame parasvānāmanādānamalobha iti kīrtyate  BndP maithunasyāsamācāro na cintā nānujalpanam nivṛttirbrahmacaryaṃ tadacchidraṃ tapa ucyate  BndP ātmārthaṃ vā parārthaṃ vā cendriyāṇīha yasya vai mithyā na saṃpravarttante śāmasyaitattu lakṣamam  BndP daśātmake yo viṣaye kāraṇe cāṣṭalakṣaṇe na kruddhyeta pratihataḥ sa jitātmā vibhāvyate  BndP yadyadiṣṭatamaṃ dravyaṃ nyāyenaivāgataṃ ca yat tattadguṇavate deyamityetaddānalakṣaṇam  BndP dānaṃ trividhamityetatkaniṣṭhajyeṣṭhamadhyamam tatra naiśreyasaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ kaniṣṭhaṃ svārthasiddhaye  BndP kāruṇyātsarvabhūteṣu saṃvibhāgastu madhyamaḥ śrutismṛtibhyāṃ vihito dharmo varmāśramātmakaḥ  BndP śiṣṭācārāviruddhaśca dharmaḥ satsādhusaṃmataḥ apradveṣohyani ṣṭeṣu tatheṣṭasyābhinandanam  BndP prītitāpaviṣādebhyo vinivṛttirviraktatā saṃnyāsaḥ karmaṇāṃ nyāsaḥ kṛtānāmakṛtaiḥ saha  BndP kuśalākuśalānāṃ tu prahāṇaṃ nyāsa ucyate vyaktā ye viśeṣāste vikāre sminnacetane  BndP cetanācetanānyatvavijñānaṃ jñānamucyate pratyaṅgānāṃ tu dharmasya tvityetallakṣaṇaṃ smṛtam  BndP ṛṣibhirdharmatattvajñaiḥ pūrvaṃ svāyaṃbhuve ntare atra vo varṇayiṣyāmi vidhiṃ manvantarasya yaḥ  BndP tathaiva cāturhetrasya cāturvidyasya caiva hi pratimanvantare caiva śrutiranyā vidhīyate  BndP ṛco yajūṃṣi samāni yathā ca pratidaivatam ābhūtasaṃplavasyāpi varjyaikaṃ śatarudriyam  BndP vidhirhaitrastathā stotraṃ pūrvavatsaṃpravartate dravyastotraṃ guṇastotraṃ phalastotraṃ tathaiva ca  BndP caturthamābhijanakaṃ stotrametaccaturvidham manvantareṣu sarveṣu yathā devā bhavanti ye  BndP pravartayati teṣāṃ vai brahmā stotraṃ caturvidham evaṃ mantragaṇānāṃ tu samutpattiścaturvidhā  BndP atharvagaryajuṣāṃ sāmnāṃ vedeṣviha pṛthakpṛthak ṛṣīṇāṃ tapyatāmugraṃ tapaḥ paramaduṣkaram  BndP mantrāḥ prādurbabhūvurhi pūrvamanvantareṣviha asaṃtoṣādbhayā dduḥkhātsukhācchokācca pañcadhā  BndP ṛṣīṇāṃ tārakākhyena darśanena yadṛcchayā ṛṣīṇāṃ yadṛṣitvaṃ hi tadvakṣyāmīha lakṣaṇaiḥ  BndP atītānāgatānāṃ ca pañcadhā tvṛṣirucyate atastvṛṣīṇāṃ vakṣyāmi tatra hyārṣasamudbhavam  BndP guṇasāmye varttamāne sarvasaṃpralaye tadā avibhāge tu vedānāmanirdeśye tamomaye  BndP abuddhibūrvakaṃ tadvai cetanārthe pravarttate cetanābuddhipūrvaṃ tu cetanena pravarttate  BndP pravarttate tathā dvau tu yathā matsyodake ubhe cetanādhiṣṭhitaṃ sattvaṃ pravarttati guṇātmakam  BndP kāraṇatvāttathā kāryaṃ tadā tasya pravarttate viṣayo viṣayitvācca artherthatvāttathaiva ca  BndP kālena prāpaṇīyena bhedāstu karaṇātmakāḥ saṃsidhyanti tadā vyaktāḥ krameṇa mahadādayaḥ  BndP mahataścāpyahaṅkārastasmādbhūtedriyāṇi ca bhūtabhedāśca bhūtebhyo jajñire sma parasparam  BndP saṃsiddhakāryakaraṇaḥ sadya eva vyavarttata yatholmukāttu truṭayaḥ ekakālādbhavanti hi  BndP tathā vivṛttāḥ kṣetrajñāḥ kālenaikena kāraṇāt yathāndhakāre khadyotaḥ sahasā saṃpradṛśyate  BndP tathā vivṛtto hyavyaktātkhadyota iva sañjvalan sa māhansaśarīrastu yatraivāyamavarttata  BndP tatraiva saṃsthito vidvāndvāraśālāmukhe vibhuḥ mahāṃstu tamasaḥ pāre vailakṣaṇyādvibhāvyate  BndP tatraiva saṃsthite vidvāṃstamasoṃta iti śrutiḥ buddhirvivarttamānasya prādurbhūtā caturvidhā  BndP jñānaṃ vairāgyamaiśvaryaṃ dharmaśceti catuṣṭayam sāṃsiddhikānyathaitāni vijñeyāni narasya vai  BndP sa mahātmā śarīrasya vaivarttātsiddhirucyate anuśete yataḥ sarvānkṣetrajñānamathāpi vā  BndP puriṣatvācca puruṣaḥ kṣatrejñānātsa ucyate yasmādvuddhyānuśete ca tasmādvodhātmakaḥ sa vai  BndP saṃsiddhaye parigataṃ vyaktāvyaktamacetanam evaṃ vivṛttaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ kṣetrajñānābhisaṃhitaḥ  BndP vivṛttisamakālaṃ tu buddhyāvyaktamṛṣiḥ svayam paraṃ hyarṣayate yasmātparamarṣitvamasya tat  BndP gatyarthādṛṣaterdhātornāma nirvṛtirāditaḥ yasmādeva svayaṃ bhūtastasmāccāpyṛṣitā smṛtā  BndP īśvarātsvayamudbhūtā mānasā brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ yasmādutpadyamānaistairmahānparigataḥ paraḥ  BndP yasmādaṣanti te dhīrā mahāntaṃ sarvato guṇaiḥ tasmānmaharṣayaḥ proktā buddheḥ parama darśinā  BndP īśvarāṇāṃ sutāsteṣāṃ mānasā aurasāśca vai ahaṅkāraṃ tapaścaiva ṛṣanti ṛṣitāṃ gatāḥ  BndP tasmātsaptarṣayaste vai bhūtādau tattvadarśanāt ṛṣiputrā ṛṣīkāstu maithunādgarbhasaṃbhavāḥ  BndP tanmātrāṇi ca satyaṃ ca ṛṣante te mahaujasaḥ saptaṣaryasta taste ca parasatyasya darśanāḥ  BndP ṛṣīkāṇāṃ sutāste syurvijñeyā ṛṣiputrakāḥ ṛṣanti te ṛtaṃ yasmādviśeṣāṃścaiva tattvataḥ  BndP tasmātsaptarṣayastepi śruteḥ paramadarśanāt avyaktātmā mahānātmāhaṅkārātmā tathaiva ca  BndP bhūtātmā cendriyātmā ca teṣāṃ tajjñānamucyate ityetā ṛṣijātīstā nāmabhiḥ pañca vai śṛṇu  BndP bhṛgurmarīciratriśca hyaṅgirāḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ manurdakṣo vasiṣṭaśca pulastyaśceti te daśa  BndP brahmaṇo mānasā hyete udbhūtāḥ svayamīśvarāḥ paratvenarṣayo yasmātsmṛtāstasmānmaharṣayaḥ  BndP īśvarāṇāṃ sutā hyete ṛṣayastānnibodhata kāvyo bṛhaspatiścaiva kaśyapaśvyavanastathā  BndP utathyo vāmadevaśca apā syaścośijastathā kardamo viśravāḥ śaktirvālakhilyāstathārvataḥ  BndP ityete ṛṣayaḥ proktāstapasā carṣitāṃ gatāḥ ṛṣiputrānṛ ṣīkāṃstu garbhotpannānnibodhata  BndP vatsaro nagṛhūścaiva bharadvājastathaiva ca ṛṣidīrghatamāścaiva bṛhadukthaḥ śaradvataḥ  BndP vājaśravāḥ śuciścaiva vaśyāśvaśca parāśaraḥ dadhīcaḥ śaṃśapāścaiva rājā vaiśravaṇastathā  BndP ityete ṛṣikāḥ proktāste satyādṛṣitāṃ gatāḥ īśvarā ṛṣayaścaiva ṛṣikāścaiva te smṛtāḥ  BndP ete mantrakṛtaḥ sarve kṛtsnaśastānnibodhata bhṛguḥ kāvyaḥ pracetāśca ṛcīko hyātmavānapi  BndP aurvātha jamadagniśca vidaḥ sārasvatastathā ārṣṭiṣeṇo yudhājicca vītahavyasuvarcasau  BndP vainyaḥ pṛthurdivodāso bādhyaśvo gṛtsaśaunakau ekonaviśatirhyetebhṛgavo mantravāditaḥ  BndP aṅgirā vaidyagaścaiva bharadvājo tha bāṣkaliḥ ṛtavākastathā gargaḥ śiniḥ saṃkṛtireva ca  BndP purukutsaśca māndhātā hyaṃbarīṣastathaiva ca yuvanāśvaḥ paurakutsastrasaddasyuśca dasyumān  BndP āhāryo hyajamīḍhaśca tukṣayaḥ kapireva ca vṛṣādarbho virūpāśvaḥ kaṇvaścaivātha mudgalaḥ  BndP utathyaśca sanadvājastathā vājaśravā api ayāsyaścakravarttī cavāmadevastathaiva ca  BndP asijo bṛhadukthaśca ṛṣirdīrghatamāstathā kakṣīvāṃśca trayastriṃśatsmṛtā hyāṅgirasā varāḥ  BndP ete mantrakṛtaḥ sarve kāśyapāṃstu nibodhata kāśyapaścaiva vatsāro naidhruvo raibhya eva ca  BndP asito deva laścaiva ṣaḍete brahmavādinaḥ atrirarvasanaścaiva śyāvāśvaśca gaviṣṭhiraḥ  BndP āvihotra ṛṣirddhīmāṃstathā pūrvātithiśca saḥ ityete cā trayaḥ proktā mantrakārā maharṣayaḥ  BndP vasiṣṭhaścaiva śaktiśca tathaiva ca parāśaraḥ caturtha indrapramatiḥ pañcamaśca bharadvasuḥ  BndP ṣaṣṭhaśca maitrāvaruṇiḥ kuṇḍinaḥ saptamastathā iti sapta vaśiṣṭhāśca vijñeyā brahmavādinaḥ  BndP viśvāmitrastu gādheyo devarātastathodgalaḥ tathā vidvānmadhucchandā ṛṣiścānyo ghamarṣaṇaḥ  BndP aṣṭako lohitaścaiva kataḥ kolaśca tāvubhau devaśravāstathā reṇuḥ pūraṇo tha dhanañjayaḥ  BndP trayodaśaite dharmiṣṭhā vijñeyāḥ kuśikāvarāḥ agastyo yo dṛḍhāyuśca vidhmavāhastathaiva ca  BndP brahmiṣṭhāgastapā hyete trayaḥ paramakīrttayaḥ manurvaivasvataścaiva elo rājā purūkhāḥ  BndP kṣatrriyāṇāṃ carāvetau vijñeyau mantravādinau bhalandanaśca vatsaśca saṃkīlaścaiva te trayaḥ  BndP ete mantrakṛtaścaiva vaiśyānāṃ pravarāḥ smṛtāḥ ityeṣā navatiḥ proktā mantrā yairṛṣibhiḥ kṛtāḥ brāhyaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyā ṛṣiputrānnibodhata  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte pūrvabhāge dvitīye nuṣaṅgapāde yugaprajālakṣaṇamṛṣipravaravarṇanaṃ ca nāma dvātriṃśattamo dhyāyaḥsūta uvācaṛṣikāṇāṃ sutāścāpi vijñeyā ṛṣiputrakāḥ brāhyaṇānāṃ pravaktāro nāmataśca nibodhata  BndP sapradhānāḥ pravakṣyante samāsācca śrutarṣayaḥ bahvṛco bhārgavaḥ pailaḥ sāṃkṛtyo jājalistathā  BndP saṃdhyāstirmāṭharaścaiva yājñavalkyaḥ parāśaraḥ upamanyurindrapramatirmāḍūkiḥ śākaliśca saḥ  BndP bāṣkaliḥ śokapāṇiśca nailaḥ pailo lakastathā pannagāḥ pakṣagantāśca ṣaḍaśītiḥ śrutarṣayaḥ  BndP ete dvijātayo mukhyā bahvṛcānāṃ śrutarṣayaḥ vaiśaṃpāyanalauhityau kaṇṭhakālāvaśāvadhaḥ  BndP śyāmāpatiḥ palāḍuśca ālaṃbiḥ kamalāpatiḥ teṣāṃ śiṣyāḥ praśiṣyāśca ṣaḍaśīti śrutarṣayaḥ  BndP ete dvijarṣayaḥ proktāścarakādhvaryavo dvijāḥ caiminiḥ sabharadvājaḥ kāvyaḥ pauṣyañjireva ca  BndP hiraṇyanābhaḥ kauśilyo laugākṣiḥ kusumistathā laṅgalī śālihotraśca śaktirājaśca bhārgavaḥ  BndP sāmagānāmathācārya ailo rājā purūravāḥ ṣaṭcatvāriṃśadanye vai teṣāṃ śiṣyāḥ śrutarṣayaḥ  BndP kauśītiḥ kaṅkamudgaśca kuṇḍakaḥ saparāśaraḥ lobhālobhaśca dharmātmā tathā brahma balaśca saḥ  BndP kranthalo tho madagalo mārkaṇḍeyo tha dharmavit ityete navatirjñeyā hotravadbrahmacāriṇaḥ  BndP carakādhvaryavaścāpi hyanumaṃntraṃ tu brāhmaṇam calūbhiḥ sumatiścaiva tathā devavaraśca yaḥ  BndP anukṛṣṇastathāyuśca anubhūmistathaiva ca tathāprītaḥ kṛśāśvaśva sumūlirbāṣkalistathā  BndP carakādhvaryakādhvaryunamasyurbrahmacāriṇaḥ vaiyāsakiḥ śuko vidvāṃllaukirbhūriśravāstathā  BndP somāviratunāntakyastathā dhaumyaśca kāśyapaḥ āraṇyā ilakaścaiva upamanyurvidastathā  BndP bhārgavo madhukaḥ piṅgaḥ śveta ketustathaiva ca prajādarpaḥ kahoḍaśca yājñavalkyo tha śaunakaḥ  BndP anaṅgo niratālaśca madhyamādhvaryavastute aditirdevamātā ca jalāpā caiva mānavī  BndP urvaśī viśvayoṣā ca hyapsaraḥpravare śubhe mudgalā cātujīvaiva tārā caiva yaśasvinī  BndP prātimedhī ca mārgā ca sujātā ca mahātapā lopāmudrā ca dharmajñā yā ca kośītikā smṛtā  BndP etāśca brahmavādinya apsaro rūpaṃsamatāḥ ityetā mukhyaśaḥ proktā mayā ca ṛṣiputrakāḥ  BndP vaidaśākhāpraṇayanāstataste ṛṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ īśvarā mantravaktāra ṛṣayo hyṛṣikāstathā  BndP ṛṣiputrāḥ pravaktaraḥ kalpānāṃ brāhmaṇasya tu īśvarāṇāmṛṣīṇāṃ ca ṛṣikāṇāṃ sahātmajaiḥ  BndP tathā vākyāni janīṣva yathaiṣāṃ mantradṛṣṭayaḥ tatrājñāyuktamadvaitaṃ dīptaṃ gaṃbhīraśabdavat  BndP atyantamaparokṣaṃ ca liṅgaṃ nāma tathaiva ca sarvabhūtānyabhūtaṃ ca paridānaṃ ca yadbhavet  BndP kvacinniruktaproktārthaṃ vākyaṃ svāyaṃbhuvaṃ viduḥ yatkiñcinmantrasaṃyuktaṃ tatra nāmavibhaktibhiḥ  BndP pratyakṣābhihitaṃ caivamṛṣīṇāṃ vacanaṃ matam naigamairvividhaiḥ śabdairnipātairbahulaṃ ca yat  BndP yaccāpyasti mahadvākyamṛṣīkāṇāṃ vacaḥ smṛtam avispaṣṭapadaṃ yacca yacca syādbahusaṃśayam  BndP ṛṣiputravacastadvai sarvāśca paridevatāḥ hetudṛṣṭānta bahulaṃ citraśabdamapārthakam  BndP sarvāstu tamaśaktaṃ ca vākyametattu mānuṣam miśrā iti samākhyātāḥ prabhāvādṛṣitāṃ gātāḥ  BndP samutkarṣāya karṣābhyāṃ jātivyatyāsasaṃbhavāḥ bhūtabhavyabhavajjñāna janmaduḥkhacikitsanam  BndP miśrāṇāṃ tadbhavedvākyaṃ gurorbalapravarttanam dharmaśāstrapraṇetāro mahimnā sarvagāśca vai  BndP tapaḥprakarṣaḥ sumahānyeṣāṃ te ṛṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ bṛhaspatiśca śukraśca vyāsaḥ sārasvatastathā  BndP vyāsāḥ śāstrapraṇayanā vedavyāsa iti smṛtāḥ yasmādavārajāḥ saṃtaḥ pūrvebhyo medhayādhikāḥ  BndP aiśvaryeṇa ca saṃpannāstataste ṛṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ yasminkālo na caṃ vayaḥ pramāṇamṛṣibhāvane  BndP dṛśyate hi pumānkaścitkaścijjyeṣṭhatamo dhiyā yasmādbuddhyā ca varṣīyānbalo pi śrutavānṛṣiḥ  BndP yaḥ kaścitpādavānmadhye prayukto kṣara saṃpadā viniyuktāvasānāṃ tu tāmṛcaṃ paricakṣate  BndP yaḥ kaścitkaraṇairmantro na ca pādakṣarairmitaḥ atiyuktāvasānaṃ ca tadyajurvai pracakṣate  BndP hrīṅkāraḥ praṇavo gītaḥ prastāvaśca caturthakam pañcamaḥ pratihotraśca ṣaṣṭhamāhurupadravam  BndP nidhanaṃ saptamaṃ sāmnaḥ saptavindhya midaṃ smṛtam pañcavindhya iti proktaṃ hrīṅkāraḥ praṇavādṛte  BndP brahmaṇe dharmamatyuktau yattadā jñāpyaterthataḥ āśāstistu prasaṃkhyātā vilāpaḥ paridevanā  BndP krodhādvā dveṣaṇāccaiva praśrākhyānaṃ tathaiva ca etattu sarvavidyānāṃ vihitaṃ mantralakṣaṇam  BndP mantrā navavidhāḥ proktā ṛgyajuḥ sāmalakṣaṇāḥ mūrtirnindā praśaṃsā cākrośastoṣastathaiva ca  BndP praśrānujñāstathākhyānamāśāsmatividhayo matāḥ mantrabhedāṃśca vakṣyāmi caturviśatilakṣaṇān  BndP praśaṃsā stutirākrośo nindā ca paridevanā abhiśāpo viśāpaśca praśnaḥ prativacastathā  BndP āśīryajñastathākṣepa arthākhyānaṃ ca saṃkathā viyogā hyabhiyogāśca kathā saṃsthā varaśca vai  BndP pratiṣedhopa deśau ca namaskāraḥ spṛhā tathā vilāpaśceti mantrāṇāṃ caturviṃśatiruddhṛtāḥ  BndP ṛṣibhiryajñatattvajñairvihitaṃ brahmaṇaṃ purā hetu rnirvacanaṃ nindā praśastiḥ saṃśayo nidhiḥ  BndP purākṛtipurākalpau vyavadhāraṇakalpanā upamā ca daśaite vai vidhayo brāhmaṇasya tu  BndP lakṣaṇaṃ praṇaśyati vedakriyā hi kāryāḥ syurmābhūdvedavināśanam  BndP vede nāśamanuprāpte yajño nāśaṃ gamiṣyati yajñe naṣṭe vedanāśastataḥ sarvaṃ praṇaśyati  BndP ādyo vedaśca tuṣpādaḥ śatasāhasrasaṃmitaḥ
