BndP prayujyate hyaśvamedhastena vā puṣyate tu saḥ ṛco gṛhītvā pailastu vyabhajattu dvidhā punaḥ  BndP dve kṛtvā saṃhite caiva śiṣyābhyā madadādvibuḥ indrapramattaye caikāṃ dvitīyāṃ bāṣkalāya ca  BndP catasraḥ saṃhitāḥ kṛtvā bāṣkalo dvijasattamaḥ śiṣyānadhyāpayā māsa śuśruṣābhiratānhitān  BndP bodhyāṃ tu prathamāṃ śākhāṃ dvitīyāmagnimātaram pārāśarīṃ tṛtīyāṃ tu yāvalkyāmathāparām  BndP indrapramatirekāṃ tu saṃhitāmṛṣisattamaḥ adhyāpayanmahābhāgaṃ māṇḍūkeyaṃ yaśasvinam  BndP styasravasamagryaṃ tu putraṃ sa tu mahāyaśāḥ satyasravāḥ satyahitaṃ putramadhyāpayadvibhuḥ  BndP so pi prathamasteṣāṃ tasmādanyo rathītaraḥ bāṣkaliśca bharadvāja iti śākhāpravarttakāḥ  BndP devamitrastu śākalyo jñānāhaṅkāragarvitaḥ janakasya sa yajñe vai vināśāmagamaddvijāḥ  BndP śāṃśapāyana mahāsāraṃ dhanagṛdhnā jighṛkṣavaḥ āhvayāñcakrire nyonyaṃ vedajñānamadolbaṇān  BndP manasā gatavittāste mamaitaddhanamityuta mamaitanna tavetyanyo brūhi vā kiṃ vikatthase  BndP ityevaṃ dhanadoṣeṇa samudra iva saṃplave tānuvāca tataḥ svastho yājñavalkyo hasanniva  BndP krodhaṃ mā kārṣṭa vidvāṃso bhavantaḥ satyavādinaḥ vadāmahe yathāśakti jijñāsaṃtaḥ parasparam  BndP tato bhyupagatāsteṣāṃ vādāḥ nāgaccheddvijasattamaḥ sa kuryādbrahmahatyāṃ vai samayo naḥ prakīrtitaḥ  BndP tataste sagaṇāḥ sarve vaiśaṃpāyanavarjitāḥ prayayuḥ saptarātreṇa yatra saṃdhiḥ kṛto bhavat  BndP brahmaṇānāṃ tu vacanādbrahmahatyāṃ cakāra saḥ śiṣyānatha samānīya sa vaiśaṃpāyano bravīt  BndP brahmahatyāṃ caradhvaṃ vai matkṛte dvijasattamāḥ sarve yūyaṃ samāgamya brūta kāmaṃ hitaṃ vacaḥ  BndP yājñavalkya uvācaahamekaścariṣyāmi tiṣṭhantu munayastvime balenotthāpayiṣyāmi tapasā svena bhāvitaḥ  BndP eva muktastataḥ kruddho yāvalkyama thātyajat uvāca yattvayādhītaṃ sarvaṃ pratyarpayasva me  BndP evamuktaḥ sarūpāṇi yajūṃṣi gurave dadau rudhireṇa tathāktāni ccharditvā brahmavittamāḥ  BndP tataḥ sa dhyānamāsthāya saryamārādhayaddvijaḥ sūrye brahma yadutpannaṃ taṃ gatvā pratitiṣṭhati  BndP tato yāni gatānyūrdhvaṃ yajūṣyādityamaḍalam tāni tasmai dadau tuṣṭaḥ sūryo vai brahmarātaye  BndP aśvarūpāya mārttaṇḍo yājñavaklyāya dhīmate yajūṃṣyadhīyate tāni brāhmaṇā yena kenacit  BndP aśvarūpāya dattāni śatamekādhikaṃ jñeyaṃ yajuṣāṃ ye vikalpakāḥ  BndP putramadhyāpayāmāsa sumantumatha jaiminiḥ sumantuścāpi sutvānaṃ putramadhyāpayatpunaḥ  BndP sukarmāṇaṃ tataḥ sunvānputramadhyāpayatpunaḥ sa BndP trayastu kuśumeḥ śiṣyā aurasaḥ sa parāśaraḥ  BndP nābhirvittastu tejasvī trividhā kauśumāḥ smṛtāḥ śauriṣuḥ śṛṅgiputraśca dvāvetau tu ciravratau  BndP rāṇāyanīyiḥ saumitriḥ sāmavedaviśāradau provāca saṃhitāsti sraḥ śṛṅgiputrau mahātpāḥ  BndP vainaḥ prājīnayogaśca surālaśca dvijauttamaḥ provāca saṃhitāḥ ṣaṭtu pārāśaryastu kauthumaḥ  BndP āsurāyaṇavaiśākhyau vedavṛddhaparāyaṇau prācīnayogaputraśca buddhimāṃśca patañjaliḥ  BndP kauthumasya tu bhedāśca pārāśaryasya paṭ samṛtāḥ lāṅgalaḥ śālihotraśca ṣaḍuvācātha saṃhitāḥ  BndP hālinirjyāmahāniśca jaiminirlomagāyaniḥ kaṇḍuśca kohalaścaiva ṣaḍe te lāṅgalāḥ smṛtāḥ  BndP ete lāṅgalinaḥ śiṣyāḥ saṃhitā yaiḥ pravarttitāḥ eko hiraṇyanābhasya kṛtaḥ śiṣyo nṛpātmajaḥ  BndP so karottu caturviśasaṃhitā dvipadāṃ varaḥ provāca caiva parikīrttitau  BndP pauṣyañjiśca kṛtaścaiva saṃhitānāṃ vikalpakau atharvāṇaṃ dvidhā kṛtvā sumanturadadāddvijāḥ  BndP kabandhāya punaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ sa ca vidvānyathāśrutam kabandhastu dvidhā kṛtvā pathyāyaikaṃ punardadau  BndP dvitīyaṃ devadarśāyasa caturdhākarotprabhuḥ modo brahmabalaścaiva pippalādastathaiva ca  BndP śaulkāyaniśca dharmajñaścaturthastapasi sthitaḥ devadarśasya catvāraḥ śiṣyā BndP savālakhilyāḥ saptaitāḥ sasuparṇāḥ prakīrttitāḥ aṣṭau sāmasahasrāṇi sāmāni ca caturddaśa  BndP sāraṇyakaṃ sahohaṃ ca etadgāyanti sāmagāḥ dvādaśaiva sahasrāṇi cchanda ādhvaryavaṃ smṛtam  BndP mantrotpattiḥ punaḥ punaḥ dvāpareṣu punarbhedāḥ śrutīnāṃ parikīrttitāḥ  BndP evaṃ vedaṃ tadāpyasya bhagavānṛṣisattamaḥ śiṣcebyaśca pradattvā tu tapastaptu vana gataḥ  BndP tasya śiṣyapraśiṣyaistu śākhābhedāstvime kṛtāḥ aṅgāni vedāścatvāro mīmāṃsā nyāyavistaraḥ  BndP dharmaśāstraṃ purāṇaṃ ca vidyāścemāścaturdaśa āyurvedo dhanurvedo gāndharvaśceti te trayaḥ  BndP arthaśāstraṃ caturthaṃ tu vidyā BndP paryāyakāle saṃprāpte saṃbhūtā nidhanasya te avaśyabhāvinārthena saṃbhadhyante tadā tu te  BndP tataste doṣavajjanma paśyanto rogapūrvakam nivarttate tadā vṛttiḥ sā teṣāṃ doṣadarśanāt  BndP evaṃ yathāvadvinivarttate  BndP etasminnantare pūrvaṃ trailākyasye śvarāstu ye saptarṣayaśca devāśca pitaro manavastathā  BndP manvantarasya kāle tu saṃpūrṇe sādhike tadā kṣīṇe dhikāre saṃvignā buddhvā manvantareśvarāḥ  BndP devatāḥ pitaraścaiva ṛṣayo manureva ca manvantare tu saṃpūrṇe tadvadante kalau yuge  BndP saṃpadyate kṛtaṃ teṣu kaliśiṣṭeṣu vai tadā yathā kṛtasya saṃtānaḥ kalipūrvaḥ smṛto budhaiḥ  BndP tathā manvantarānteṣu ādirmanvantarasya ca kṣīṇe manvantare pūrve pravṛtte cāpare punaḥ  BndP mukhe kṛtayugasyātha teṣāṃ śiṣṭāstu ye tadā saptarṣayo manuścaiva kālāpekṣāstu ye sthitāḥ  BndP manvantarapratīkṣāste kṣīyamāṇāstapasvinaḥ manvantarotsavasyārthe saṃtatyarthe ca sarvadā  BndP pūrvavatsaṃpravarttante pravṛtte vṛṣṭisarjane dvandveṣu saṃpravṛtteṣu utpannāsvauṣadhīṣu ca  BndP prajāsu cāniketāsu saṃsthitāsu kvacitkvacit vārttāyāṃ saṃpravṛttāyāṃ dharme caivopasaṃsthite  BndP nirānande cāpi loke naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame agrāmanagare caiva varṇāśramavivarjite  BndP pūrvamanvantare śiṣṭā ye bhavantīha dhārmikāḥ saptarṣayo manuścaiva saṃtānārthaṃ vyavasthitāḥ  BndP prajārthaṃ tapatāṃ teṣāṃ tapaḥ paramaduścaram utpadyante hi pūrveṣāṃ nidhaneṣviha pūrvavat  BndP devāsurāḥ pitṛgaṇā ṛṣayo mānuṣāstathā sarpā bhūtapiśācāśca gandharvā yakṣarākṣasāḥ  BndP tatasteṣāṃ tu ye śiṣṭāḥ śiṣṭācārānprajakṣate saptarṣayo manuścava hyādau manvantarasya hi  BndP prārabhante ca karmāṇi manuṣyo daivataiḥ saha ṛṣīṇāṃ brahmacaryeṇa gatvānṛṇyaṃ tu va tadā  BndP pitṝṇāṃ prajāyā caiva devānāmijyayā tathā śataṃvarṣasahasrāṇāṃ dharme varṇātmake sthitāḥ  BndP trayī vārttā daṇḍanītirdharmānvarṇāśramāṃstathā sthāpayitvāśramāṃścaiva svargāya dedhire manaḥ  BndP pūrvadeveṣu teṣvevaṃ svargāyā bhimukheṣu vai pūrvadevāstataste vai sthitā dharmeṇa kṛtsnaśaḥ  BndP manvantare purāvṛtte sthānānyutsṛjya sarvaśaḥ mantraiḥ sahordhvaṃ gacchanti maharlokamanāmayam  BndP vinivṛttādhikārāste mānasīṃ siddhimāsthitāḥ avekṣamāṇā vaśinastiṣṭhantyā bhūtasaṃplavāt  BndP tatasteṣu vyatīteṣu pūrvadeveṣu vai tadā śūnyeṣu devasthāneṣu trailokye teṣu sarvaśaḥ  BndP upasthitā ihānye vai ye devāḥ svargavāsinaḥ tataste tapasā yuktāḥ sthānānyāpūrayanti ca  BndP satyena brahmacaryeṇa śrutena ca samanvitāḥ saptarṣīṇāṃ manoścaiva devānāṃ pitṛbhiḥ saha  BndP nidhanānīha pūrveṣāmāditāṃ ca bhaviṣyatām teṣāṃ saṃtatyaviccheda ihāmanvantarakṣayāt  BndP evaṃ pūrvānupūrvyeṇa sthitisteṣāmavasthitā manvantareṣu sarveṣu yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam  BndP pūrvamanvantarāṇāṃ tu pratisaṃdhānalakṣaṇam atītānāgatānāṃ vai proktaṃ svāyaṃbhuvena tu  BndP manvantareṣvatīteṣu bhaviṣyāṇāṃ tu sādhanam evaṃ saṃtatyavicchedo bhavatyābhūtasaṃplavāt  BndP manvantarāṇāṃ parivarttanāni hyekāntatastāni mahargatāni mahājanaṃ caiva janāntapaśca caikāntagāni prabhavanti satye  BndP tadbhāvināṃ tatra tu darśanena nānātvadṛṣṭena ca pratyayena stye sthitā nityatayā tu nityaṃ prāpte vikāre pratisarga kāle  BndP manvantarāṇāṃ parivarttanāni muñcanti satyaṃ tu tato parānta tato bhiyogā viṣayaprahāṇādviśanti nārāyaṇameva devam  BndP manvantarāṇāṃ parivarttaneṣu cirapravṛtteṣu vidhisvabhāvāt kṣaṇaṃ na vai tiṣṭhati jīvalokaḥ kṣayodayābhyāṃ parivartamānaḥ  BndP ityantarāṇyevamṛṣistutānāṃ dharmātmanāṃ divyadṛśāṃ manūnām vāyupraṇītānyupalabhya dṛśyād divyaujasāṃ vyāsasamāsayogaiḥ  BndP sarvāṇi rājarṣisurarthimanti brahmarṣidevoragavanti caiva sureśasaptarṣipitṛprajeśairyuktāni samyak parivarttanāni  BndP udāravaṃśābhijana śrutīnāṃ prakṛṣṭamedhābhisamedhitānām kīrtidyutikhyātibhirarcitānāṃ puṇyaṃ hi viśyāpanamīśvarāṇām  BndP svargīyametatparamaṃ pavitraṃ putrīyametacca paraṃ rahasyam japyaṃ mahāparvasu caitadagryaṃ duḥkhāpaśāntipradamāyuṣīyam  BndP prajaśadavarṣimanupradhānāṃ puṇyāṃ prasūtiṃ prathitāmajasya mamāpi vikhyāpayataḥ samāsātsiddhiṃ prajeśāḥ pradiśantu yuktāḥ  BndP ityetadantaraṃ proktaṃ manoḥ svāyaṃbhuvasya ca vistareṇānupūrvyā ca bhūyaḥ kiṃ varṇayāmyaham  BndP  iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte pūrvabhāge dvitīye nuṣgapāde vedavyasanākhyānaṃ svāyaṃbhuvamanvantaravarṇanaṃ ca nāma pañcatriṃśattamo śāṃśapāyana uvācamanvantarāṇi śeṣāṇi śrotumicchāmyanukramāt manvantarādhipāṃścaiva śakradevapurogamān  BndP sūta uvācamanvantarāṇi yāni syuratītānāgatāni ha samāsā dvistarāccaiva bruvato me nibodhata  BndP svāyaṃbhuvo manuḥ pūrvaṃ manuḥ svārociṣastathā uttamastāmasaścaiva raivataścākṣuṣastathā  BndP ṣaḍete manavo tītā vakṣyāmyaṣṭāvanāgatān sāvarṇiścaiva raucyaśca bhautyo vaivasvatastathā  BndP vakṣyāmyetānpurastāttu manorvevasvatasya ca manavaḥ pañca ye tītā mānasāṃstānnibodhata  BndP manvantaraṃ mayā vo dhya krāntaṃ svāyaṃbhuvasya ha ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi manāḥ svārociṣasya ha  BndP prajāsargaṃ samāsena dvitīyasya mahātmanaḥ āsanvai tuṣitā devā manoḥ svārociṣe ntare  BndP pārāvatāśca vidvāṃso dvāveva tu gaṇau smṛtau tuṣitāyāṃ samutpannāḥ kratoḥ putrāḥ svarociṣaḥ  BndP pārāvatāśca vāsiṣṭhā dvādaśa dvau gaṇau smṛtau chandajāśca caturviṃśaddevāste vai tadā smṛtāḥ  BndP divasparśo tha jāmitro gopado bhāsurastathā ajaśca bhagavāścaiva draviṇaśya mahā balaḥ  BndP āyaścāpi mahābāhurmahaujāścāpi vīryavān cikitvānviśruto yastu cāṃśo yaścaiva paṭhyate  BndP ṛtaścadvādaśasteṣāṃ tuṣitāḥ parikīrttitāḥ ityete kratuputrāstu tadāsansomapāyinaḥ  BndP pracetāścaiva yo devo viśvadevastathaiva ca samañjo viśruto yastu hyajihmaścārimarddanaḥ  BndP āyurdāno mahāmāno divyamānastathaiva ca ajeyaśca mahābhāgo yavīyāṃśca mahābalaḥ  BndP hotā yajvā tathā hyete parikrāntāḥ parāvatāḥ ityetā devatā hyāsanmanoḥ svārociṣāntare  BndP somapāstu tadā hyetāścaturviśati devatāḥ teṣāmindrastadā hyāsīdvipaścillokaviśrutaḥ  BndP ūrjā vasiṣṭhaputraśca staṃbaḥ kāśyapa eva ca bhārgavaśca tadhā prāma ṛṣabhoṃṅgirasastathā  BndP paulastyaścaiva datto trirātreyo niścalastathā paulaho thārvarīvāṃśca ete saptarṣayastathā  BndP caitraḥ kiṃpuruṣa ścaiva kṛtānto vibhṛto raviḥ bṛhaduktho navaḥ setuḥ śrutaśceti nava smṛtāḥ  BndP manoḥ svārociṣasyaite putrā vaṃśakarāḥ prabho purāṇe parisaṃkhyātā dvitīyaṃ vai tadantaram  BndP saptarṣayo manurdevāḥ pitaraśca catuṣṭayam mūlaṃ manvantarasyaite teṣāṃ caivānvayāḥ prajāḥ  BndP ṛṣīṇāṃ devatāḥ putrāḥ pitaro devasūnavaḥ ṛṣayo devaputrāśca iti śāstre viniścayaḥ  BndP manoḥ kṣatraṃ viśaścaiva saptarṣibhyo dvijā tayaḥ etanmanvantaraṃ proktaṃ samāsācca na vistarāt  BndP svāyaṃbhuve na vistāro jñeyaḥ svārociṣasya ca na śakyo vistarastasya vaktuṃ varṣaśatairapi  BndP punaruktabahutvāttu prajānāṃ vai kulekule tṛtīye tvatha paryāye uttamasyāntare manoḥ  BndP pañca devagaṇā proktāstānvakṣyāmi nibodhata sudhāmānaśca ye devā ye cānye vaśavarttinaḥ  BndP pratardanāḥ śivāḥ satyāgaṇā dvādaśakāḥ smṛtāḥ satyo dhṛtirdamo dāntaḥ kṣamaḥ kṣāmo dhvaniḥ śuciḥ  BndP iṣorjjaśca tathā śreṣṭhaḥ suparṇo dvādaśastathā ityete dvādaśa proktāḥ sudhāmānastu nāmabhiḥ  BndP sahasradhāro viśvāyuḥ samitāro vṛhadvasuḥ viśvadhā viśvakarmā ca mānasastu virājasaḥ  BndP jyotiścaiva vibhāsaśca kīrttitā vaṃśavartinaḥ avadhyo varatirdevo vasurdhiṣṇyo vibhāvasuḥ  BndP vittaḥ kratuḥ sudharmā ca dhṛtadharmā yaśasvijaḥ rathormiḥ ketumāñchcaiva kīrttitāstu pratardanāḥ  BndP haṃsasvārau vadānyau ca pratardanayaśaskarau sudāno vasudānaśca sumañjasaviṣāvubhau  BndP yamo vahnir yatiścaiva sucitraḥ sutapāstathā śivā hyete tu vijñeyā yajñiyā dvādaśāparāḥ  BndP satyānāmapi nāmāni nibodhata yathātatham dikpatirvākpatiścaiva viśvaḥ śaṃbhustathaiva ca  BndP svamṛḍīko diviścaiva varcodhāmā bṛhadvapuḥ aśvaścaiva sadaśvaśca kṣemānandau tathaiva ca  BndP satyā hyete parikrāntā yajñiyā dvādaśāparāḥ ityetā devatā hyāsannauttamasyāntare manoḥ  BndP teṣāmindrastu devānāṃ suśāntirnāma viśrutaḥ putrāsttavaṅgirasaste vai uttamasya prajāpateḥ  BndP vaśiṣṭhaputrāḥ saptāsanvāśiṣṭhā iti viśrutāḥ saptarṣayastu te sarva uttamasyāntare manoḥ  BndP ācaśca paraśuścaiva divyo divyauṣadhirnayaḥ devāmvujaścāpratimau mahotsāho gajastathā  BndP vinītaśca suketuśca sumitraḥ sumatiḥ śrutiḥ uttamasya manoḥ putrāstrayodaśa mahātmanaḥ  BndP ete kṣatrapraṇetārastṛtīyaṃ caitadantaram auttamaḥ parisaṃkhyātaḥ sargaḥ svārociṣeṇa tu  BndP vistareṇānupūrvyā ca tāmasasya nibodhata caturthe tvatha paryāye tāmasasyātare manoḥ  BndP satyāḥ surūpāḥ sudhiyo harayaśca gaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ pulastyaputrāste devāstāmasasyāntare manoḥ  BndP gaṇastu teṣāṃ devānāmekaikaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ indriyāṇāṃ pratīyeta ṛṣayaḥ pratijānate  BndP sapramāṇāstu śīrṣaṇyaṃ manaścaivāṣṭamaṃ tathā indriyāṇi tathā devā manostasyāntare smṛtāḥ  BndP teṣāṃ babhūva devānāṃ śibirindraḥ pratāpavān saptarṣayoṃtare ye ca tānnibodhata sattamāḥ  BndP kāvya āṅgirasaścaiva kāśyapaḥ pṛthureva ca atreyastvagnirityeva jyotirdhāmā ca bhārgavaḥ  BndP paulahaścarakaścātra vāśiṣṭhaḥ pīvarastathā caitrastathaiva paulastya ṛṣayastāmaseṃtare  BndP jānujaṅghastathā śāntirnaraḥ khyātiḥ śubhastathā priyabhṛtyo parīkṣicca prasthalo tha dṛḍheṣudhiḥ  BndP kṛśāśvaḥ kṛtabandhuśca tāmasasya manoḥ sutāḥ pañcametvatha paryāye manoḥ svārociṣeṃtare  BndP guṇāstu ye samākhyātā devānāṃ tānnibodhata amitābhā bhūtarayo vaikuṇṭhāḥ sasumedhasaḥ  BndP variṣṭhāśca śubhāḥ putrā vasiṣṭhasya prajāpateḥ caturdaśa tu catvāro gaṇāsteṣāṃ subhāsvarāḥ  BndP ugraḥ prajño gnibhāvaśca prajyotiścāmṛtastathā sumatirvā virāvaśca dhāmā nādaḥ śravāstathā  BndP vṛttirāśī ca vādaśca śabaraśca caturdaśa amitābhāḥ smṛtā hyete devāḥ svārociṣeṃtare  BndP matiśca sumatiścaiva ṛtasatyau tathaidhanaḥ adhṛtirvidhṛtiścaiva damo niyama eva ca  BndP vrato viṣṇuḥ sahaścaiva dyutimānsuśravāstathā ityetānīha nāmāni ābhūtayasāṃ viduḥ  BndP vṛṣo bhettā jayo bhīmaḥ śucirdānto yaśo damaḥ nātho vidvānajeyaśca kṛśo gauro dhruvastathā  BndP kīrttitāstu vikuṇṭhā vai sumedhāṃstu nibodhata medhā medhā tithiścaiva satyamedhāstathaiva ca  BndP pṛśnimedhālpamedhāśca bhūyomedhāśca yaḥ prabhuḥ dīptimedhā yaśomedhā sthiramedhāstathaiva ca  BndP sarvamedhā sumedhāśca pratimedhāśca yaḥ smṛtaḥ medhajā medhahantā ca kīrttitāste sumedhasaḥ  BndP vibhurindrastathā teṣāmāsīdvi krāntapauruṣaḥ paulastyo davabāhuśca sudhāmā nāma kāśyapaḥ  BndP hiraṇyaromāṅgiraso vedaśrīścaiva bhārgavaḥ ūrdhvabāhuśca vāśiṣṭhaḥ parjanyaḥ paulahastathā  BndP satyanetrastathātreya ṛṣayo raivateṃtare mahāvīryaḥ susaṃbhāvyaḥ satyako harahā śuciḥ  BndP balabandhurnirāmitraḥ kaṃbuḥ śṛgo dhṛtavrataḥ raivatasya ca putrāste pañcamaṃ vai tadantaram  BndP svārociṣaścottamo pi tāmaso raivatastathā priyavratānvayā hyete catvāro manavaḥ smṛtāḥ  BndP ṣaṣṭhe khalvapi paryāye devā ye cākṣuṣeṃtare ādyāḥ prasūtā bhāvyaśca pṛthukāśca divaukasaḥ  BndP mahānubhāvā lekhāscha pañca devagaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ divaukasaḥ sarva eva procyante mātṛnāmabhiḥ  BndP atreḥ putrasya naptāro hyāraṇyasya prajāpateḥ gaṇastu teṣāṃ devānāmekaiko hyaṣṭakaḥ smṛtaḥ  BndP antarikṣo vasurhavyo hyatithiśca priyavrataḥ śrotā mantānumantā ca tvādyā hyete prakīrttitāḥ  BndP śyenabhadrastathā caiva śvetacakṣurmahāyaśāḥ sumanāśca pracetāśca vanenaḥ supracetsau  BndP muniścaiva mahāsattvaḥ prasūtāḥ parikīrttitāḥ vijayaḥ sujayaścaiva manasyodau tathaiva ca  BndP matiḥ parimatiścaiva vicetāḥ priyaniścayaḥ bhavyā hyete smṛtā devāḥ pṛthukāṃśca nibodhata  BndP ojiṣṭhaḥ śakuno devo vānatdṛṣṭastathaiva ca satkṛtaḥ satyadṛṣṭiśca jigīṣurvijayastathā  BndP ajitaśca mahābhāgaḥ pṛthukāste divaukasaḥ leśāstathā pravakṣyāmi nāmatastānnibodhata  BndP manojavaḥ praghāsaśca pracetāśca mahāyaśāḥ dhruvo dhruvakṣitiścaiva atyutaścaiva vīryavān  BndP yuvanā bṛhaspatiścaiva lekhāḥ saṃparikīrttitāḥ manojavo mahāvīryasteṣāmindrastadābhavat  BndP uttamo bhārgavaścaiva haviṣmānaṅgiraḥsutaḥ sudhāmā kāśyapaścaiva vaśiṣṭho virajāstathā  BndP atināmā ca paulastyaḥ sahiṣṇuḥ paulahastathā madhurātreya ityete sapta vai cākṣuṣeṃtare  BndP ūruḥ puruḥ śatadyumnastapasvī satyavākkṛtiḥ agniṣṭudatirātraśca sudyumnaśaceti te nava  BndP abhimanyuśca daśamo nāḍvaleyā manoḥ sutāḥ cākṣuṣasya sutāḥ hyete ṣaṣṭhaṃ caiva tadantaram  BndP vaivasvatena saṃkhyātastatsargaḥ sāṃpratena tu vistareṇānupūrvyā ca cākṣuṣasyāntare manoḥ  BndP ṛṣaya ūcuḥcākṣuṣaḥ kasya dāyādaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ sakya vānvaye tasyānvavāye ye pyanyetānno brūhi yathātatham  BndP sūta uvācacākṣuṣasya visargaṃ tu samāsācchṛṇuta dvijāḥ yasyānvavāye saṃbhūtaḥ pṛthurvainyaḥ pratāpavān  BndP prajānāṃ patayaścānye dakṣaḥ prācetasastathā uttānapādaṃ jagrāha putramatriprajāpatiḥ  BndP dattakaḥ sa tu putro sya rājā hyāsītprajāpatiḥ svāyaṃbhuvena manunā datto treḥ kāraṇaṃ prati  BndP manvantaramathāsādya bhaviṣyaccākṣuṣasya ha ṣaṣṭhaṃ tadanu vakṣyāmi upoddhātena vai dvijāḥ  BndP uttānapādāccaturaḥ sūnṛtāsūta bhāminī dharmasya kanyā suśroṇī sūnṛtā nāma viśrutā  BndP utpannā jāpi dharmema dhruvasya jananī śubhā dharmasya patnyāṃ lakṣmayāṃ vai utpannā sā śucismitā  BndP dhruvaṃ ca kīrttimantaṃ ca tvāyuṣmantaṃ vasuṃ tathā uttānapādo janayatkanye dve ca śucismite  BndP svarāmanasvinī caiva tayoḥ putrāḥ prakīrttitāḥ dhruvo varṣasahasrāṇi daśa divyāni vīryavān  BndP tapastepe nirāhāraḥ prārthayanvipulaṃ yaśaḥ tretāyuge tu prathame pautraḥ svāyaṃbhuvasya tu  BndP ātmānaṃ dhārayanyogānprārthayansumahadyaśaḥ tasmai brahmā dadau prīto jyotiṣāṃ sthānamuttamam  BndP ābhūtasaṃplavāddivyamastodayavivārjitam tasyātimātrāmṛddhiṃ ca mahimānaṃ nirīkṣya tu  BndP daityā surāṇāmācāryaḥ ślokamapyuśānā jagau aho sya tapaso vīryamaho śrutamaho vratam  BndP kṛtvā yadenamupari dhruvaṃ saptarṣayaḥ sthitāḥ druve tridivamāsaktamīśvaraḥ sa divaspatiḥ  BndP dhruvātsṛṣṭiṃ ca bhavyaṃ ca bhūmistau suṣuve nṛpau svāṃ chāyāmāha vai sṛṣṭirbhavanārīti tāṃ prabhuḥ  BndP satyābhivyahṛtestasya sadyaḥ strī sābhavattadā divyasaṃhananā chāyā divyābharaṇabhūṣitā  BndP chāyāyāṃ sṛṣṭirādhatta pañca putrānakalmaṣān prājīnagarbhaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ vṛkañca vṛkalaṃ dhṛtim  BndP patnī prācīnagarbhasya suvarcā suṣuve nupam nāmnodāradhiyaṃ putramindro yaḥ pūrvajanmani  BndP saṃvatsarasahasrānte sakṛdāhāramāharan evaṃ manvantaraṃ yukta indratvaṃ prāptavānprabhuḥ  BndP udāradheḥ sutaṃ bhadrājanayatsā divañjayam ripuṃ ripuñjayājjajñe varāṅgī tu divañjayāt  BndP riporādhatta bṛhatī vakṣuṣaṃ sarvatejasam tasya putro manurvidvān brahmakṣattrapravattakaḥ vyajījanatpuṣkariṇī vāruṇī cākṣuṣaṃ manum  BndP ṛṣaya ūcuḥprajāpateḥ sutā kasmādvāruṇī procyate nagha etadācakṣva tatvena kuśalo hyasi vistare  BndP sūta uvācaaraṇyasyodakaḥ putro varuṇatvamupāgataḥ tena sā vāruṇī jñeyā bhrātrā khyātimupāgatā  BndP manorajāyanta daśa naḍvalāyāṃ sutāḥ śubhāḥ kanyāyāṃ sumahāvīryā virajasya prajāpateḥ  BndP ūruḥ puruḥ śatadyumnastapasvī satyavākkṛtiḥ agniṣṭudatirātraśca sudyumnaśceti vai nava  BndP abhimanyuśca daśamo naḍvalāyāṃ manoḥ sutāḥ ūrorajanayatputrānṣaḍāgneyī mahāprabhān  BndP aṅgaṃ sumanasaṃ khyātiṅgayaṃ śukraṃ vrajājinau aṅgātsunīthāpatyaṃvai venamekaṃ vyajāyata  BndP tasyāparādhādvenasya prakopastu mahānabhūt prajārthamṛṣayo yasyamamanthurdakṣiṇāṃ karam  BndP janitastasya pāṇau tu mathite rūpavānpṛthuḥ janayitvā sutaṃ tasya pṛthuṃ prathitapauruṣam  BndP abru vaṃstveṣa vo rājā ṛṣayo muditāḥ prajāḥ sa dhanvī kavacī jajñe tejasā nirdahanniva  BndP vṛttīnāmeṣa vo dātā bhaviṣyati narādhipaḥ pṛthurvainyastadā lokānrarakṣa kṣatrapūrvajaḥ  BndP rājasūyābhiṣiktānāmādyassa vasudhādhipaḥ tasya stavārthamutpannau nipuṇau sūtamāgadhau  BndP teneyaṃ gaurmahārājñā dugdhā sasyāni dhīmatā prajānāṃ vṛttikāmānāṃ devaiścarṣigaṇaiḥ saha  BndP pitṛbhir dānavaiścaiva gandharvaiścāpsarogaṇaiḥ sarpaiḥ puṇyajanaiścaiva parvatairvṛkṣavīrudhaiḥ  BndP teṣu teṣu tu pātreṣu duhyamānā vasuṃdharā prādādyathepsi taṃ kṣīraṃ tena prāṇānadhārayan  BndP śāṃśapāyana uvācavistareṇa pṛthorjanma kīrttayasva mahāvrata yathā mahātmanā tena pūrvaṃ dugdhā vasuṃdharā  BndP yathā devaiśca nāgaiśca yathā brahmarṣibhiḥ saha yakṣai rākṣasagandharvairapsarobhiryathā purā  BndP yathā yathā ca vai sūta vidhinā yena yena ca teṣāṃ pātraviśeṣāṃśca dogdhāraṃ kṣīrameva ca  BndP tathā vatsaviśeṣāṃśca tvaṃnaḥ prabrūhi pṛcchatām yathā kṣīraviśeṣāṃśca sarvānevānupūrvaśaḥ  BndP yasmiṃśca kāraṇe pāṇirvanasya mathitaḥ purā kuddhairmaharṣibhiḥ pūrvaiḥ kāraṇaṃ brūhi taddhi naḥ  BndP sūta uvācakathayiṣyāmi vo viprāḥ pṛthorvainyasya saṃbhavam ekāgrāḥ prayatāścaiva śuśrūṣadhvaṃ dvijottamāḥ  BndP nāśuddhāya na pāpāya nāśiṣyāyāhitāya ca varttanīyamidaṃ brahma nāvratāya kathañcana  BndP dhanyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ puṇyaṃ vedaiśca saṃmitam rahasyamṛṣibhiḥ proktaṃ śṛṇuyādyo nasūyakaḥ  BndP yaścaivaṃ śrāvayenmartyaḥ pṛthorvainyasya saṃbhavam brāhmaṇebhyo namaskṛtya na sa śocetkṛtākṛtam  BndP goptā dharmasya rājāsau babhūvātrisamaḥ prabhuḥ atrivaṃśasamutpanno hyaṅgo nāma prajāpatiḥ  BndP tasya putro bhavadveno nātyarthaṃ dhārmikastathā jāto mṛtyusutāyāṃ vai sunīthāyāṃ prajāpatiḥ  BndP sa mātāmahadoṣeṇa venaḥ kālātma jātmajaḥ sa dharmaṃ vṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā kāmāllokeṣvartata  BndP sthāpanāṃ sthāpayāmāsa dharmāyetāṃ sa pārthivaḥ vedaśāstrāṇyatikramya so dharme nirato bhavat  BndP niḥsvādhyāyavaṣṭkāre tasminrājyaṃ praśāsati na pibanti tadā somaṃ mahāyajñeṣu devatāḥ  BndP na yaṣṭavyaṃ na dātavyamiti tasya prajāpateḥ āsītpratijñā krūreyaṃ vināśe pratyupasthite  BndP ahamījyaśca pūjyaśca yajñe devadvijātibhiḥ mayi yajñā vidhātavyā mayi hotavyamityapi  BndP tamatikrāntamaryādamavadānasusaṃvṛtam ūcurmaharṣayaḥ sarve marīcipramukhāstadā  BndP vayaṃ dīkṣāṃ pravekṣyāmaḥ saṃvatsaraśataṃ nṛpa tvaṃ mā kārṣīradharmaṃ vai naiṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ  BndP nidhane saṃprasūtastvaṃ prajāpatirasaṃśayaḥ pālayiṣye prajāśceti pūrvaṃ te samayaḥ kṛtaḥ  BndP tāṃ stathā vādinaḥ sarvānbrahmarṣīnabravīttadā venaḥ prahasya durbuddhirviditena ca kovidaḥ  BndP sraṣṭā dharmasya kaścānyaḥ śrotavyaṃ kasya vā mayā vīryaṇa tapasā satyairmayā vā kaḥ samo bhuvi  BndP mandātmāno na nūnaṃ māṃ yūyaṃ jānīta tattvataḥ prabhavaṃ sarvalokānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ  BndP icchandaheyaṃ pṛthivīṃ plāvayeyaṃ jalena vā sṛjeyaṃ vā graseyaṃ vā nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  BndP yadā na śakyate staṃbhādānāryyabhṛśasaṃhitaḥ anunetuṃ tadā venastataḥ kruddhā maharṣayaḥ  BndP nigṛhya taṃ ca bāhubhyāṃ visphurantaṃ mahā balam tato sya vāmahastaṃ te mamanthurbhṛśakopitāḥ  BndP tasmātpramathyamānādvai jajña pūrvamiti śrutiḥ hrasvo timātraṃ puruṣaḥ kṛṣṇaścāpi babhūva ha  BndP sa bhītaḥ prāñjaliścaiva tasthivānākulendriyaḥ tamārttaṃ vihvalaṃ dṛṣṭvā niṣīdetyabruvankila  BndP niṣādavaṃśakartāsau babhūvānantavikramaḥ dhīvarānasṛjaccāpi venakalmaṣasaṃbhavān  BndP ye cānye vindhyanilayāstaṃburāstuburāḥ khaśāḥ adharmarucayaścāpi viddhi tānvenakalmaṣān  BndP punarmaharṣayastasya pāṇiṃ venasya dakṣiṇam araṇīmiva saṃrabdhā mamanthurjātamanyavaḥ  BndP pṛthustasmātsamutpannaḥ karājjalajasannibhāt pṛthoḥ karatalādvāpi yasmājjātaḥ pṛṣustataḥ  BndP dīpyamānaśca vapuṣā sākṣādagniriva jvalan ādyamājagavaṃ nāma dhanurgṛhya mahāravam  BndP śārāṃśca bibhradrakṣārtha kavacaṃ ca mahāprabham tasmiñjā te tha bhūtāni saṃprahṛṣṭāni sarvaśaḥ  BndP samāpeturmahārājaṃ venaśca tridivaṃ gataḥ samutpannena rājarṣiḥ satputreṇa mahātmanā  BndP trātaḥ sa puruṣavyāghraḥ punnāmno narakāttadā taṃ nadyaśca samudrāśca ratnānyādāya sarvaśaḥ  BndP abhiṣekāya toyaṃ ca sarva evopata sthire pitāmahaśca bhagavānaṅgirobhiḥ sahāmaraiḥ  BndP sthāvarāṇi ca bhūtāni jaṅgamāni ca sarvaśaḥ samāgamya tadā vainyamabhya ṣiñcannarādhipam  BndP mahatā rājarājena prajāpālaṃ mahādyutim so bhiṣikto mahārājo devairaṅgirasaḥ sutaiḥ  BndP ādi rājo mahābhāgaḥ pṛthurvainyaḥ pratāpavān pitrāparañjitāstasya prajāstenānurañjitāḥ  BndP tato rājeti nāmāsya hyanurāgādajāyata āpastastaṃbhire tasya samudramabhiyāsyataḥ  BndP parvatāścāvadīryanta dhvajabhaṅgaśca nābhavat akṛṣṭapacyā pṛthivī siddhyantyannāni cintayā  BndP sarvakāmadughā gāvaḥ pṛṭake puṭake madhu etasminneva kāle tu yajatastasya vai makhe  BndP some sute samu tpannaḥ sūtaḥ sautye tadāhani tasminnevaṃ samutpanne punarjajñe tha māgadhaḥ  BndP sāmageṣu ca gāyatsu śubhāṇḍe vaiśvadevike samāgate samutpannastasmānmāgadha ucyate  BndP aindreṇa haviṣā cāpi haviḥ pṛktaṃ bṛhaspateḥ juhāvendrāya daivena tataḥ sūto vyajāyata  BndP pramādastatra saṃjajña prāyaścittaṃ ca karmasu śiṣyahavyena yatpṛktamabhibhūtaṃ gurorhaviḥ  BndP adharottaracāreṇa jajñe tadvarṇavaikṛtam yacca kṣatrātsamabhavadbrāhmaṇyāṃ hīnayonitaḥ  BndP sūtaḥ pūrveṇa sādharmyāttulyadharmaḥ prakīrttitaḥ madhyamo hyeṣa sūtasya dharmaḥ kṣetropajīvanam  BndP rathanāgāśvacaritaṃ jaghanyaṃ ca cikitsitam pṛthustavārthaṃ tau tatra samāhūtau maharṣibhiḥ  BndP tāvūcurmunayaḥ sarve stūyatāmeṣa pārthivaḥ karmaitadanurūpaṃ ca pātraṃ cāyaṃ narādhipaḥ  BndP tāvūcatustataḥ sarvāṃstānṛṣīnsūtamāgadhau āvāṃ devānṛṣīṃścaiva prīṇayāvaḥ svakarmataḥ  BndP na cāsya vidvo vai karma na tathā lakṣaṇaṃ yaśaḥ stotraṃ yenāsya kuryāva procustejasvino dvijāḥ  BndP eṣa karmarato nityaṃ satyavāksaṃyatendriyaḥ jñānaśīlo vadānyaśca saṃgrāmeṣvaparajitaḥ  BndP ṛṣibhistau niyuktau tu bhaviṣyaiḥ stūyatāmiti yāni karmāṇi kṛtavān pṛthuḥ paścānmahābalaḥ  BndP tāni gītanibaddhāni hyastutāṃ sūtamāgadhau tatastavānte suprītaḥ pṛthuḥ prādātprajeśvaraḥ  BndP anūpadeśaṃ sūtāya magadhaṃ māgadhāya ca tadādi pṛthivīpālāḥ stūyante sūtamāgadhaiḥ  BndP āśīrvādaiḥ prabodhyante sūtamāgadhabandibhiḥ taṃ dṛṣṭvā paramaprītāḥ prajā ūcurmaharṣayaḥ  BndP eṣa vṛttiprado vainyo bhaviṣyati narādhipaḥ tato vainyaṃ mahābhāgaṃ prajāḥ samabhidudruvuḥ  BndP tvaṃ no vṛttiṃ vidhatsveti mahārṣivaca nāttadā so bhidrutaḥ prajābhistu prajāhitacikīrṣayā  BndP dhanurgṛhītvā bāṇāṃśca vasudhāmādravadbalī tato vainyabhayatrastā gaurbhūtvā prādravanmahī  BndP tāṃ pṛthurdhanurādāya dravantīmanvadhāvata sā lokānbrahmalokādīngatvā vainyabhayāttadā  BndP saṃdadarśāgrato vainyaṃ kārmukodyatapāṇikam jvaladbhirniśitairbāṇairdīptatejasamacyutam  BndP mahāyogaṃ mahātmānaṃ durddharṣamamarairapi alabantī tu sā trāṇaṃ vainyamevānvapadyata  BndP kṛtāñjalipuṭā devī pūjyā lokaistribhiḥ sādā uvāca vainaṃ nādharmaḥ strīvadhe paripaśyati  BndP kathaṃ dhārayitā cāsi prajā yā varddhitā mayā mayi lokāḥ sthitā rājanmayedaṃ dhāryate jagat  BndP matkṛte na vinaśyeyuḥ prajāḥ pārthiva varddhitāḥ sa māṃ narhasi vai hantuṃ śreyastvaṃ ca cikīrṣasi  BndP prajānāṃ pṛthivīpāla śṛṇu cedaṃ vaco mama upāyataḥ samārabdhā sarve siddhyantyupakramāḥ  BndP hatvāpi māṃ na śaktastvaṃ prajānāṃ pālane nṛpa antarbhūtā bhaviṣyāmi jahi kopaṃ mahādyute  BndP avadhyaśca striyaḥ prāhustiryagyonigateṣvapi sattvaṣu pṛthivīpāla dhama na tyaktumarhasi  BndP evaṃ bahuvidhaṃ vākyaṃ śrutvā tasyā mahāmanāḥ krodhaṃ nigṛhya dharmātmā vasudhāmidamabravīt  BndP ekasyārthāya yo hanyādātmano vā parasya ca ekaṃ prāṇī bahūnvāpi karma tasyāsti pātakam  BndP yasmiṃstu nihate bhadre jīvante bahavaḥ sukham tasminhate nāsti śubhe pātakaṃ copapātakam  BndP so haṃ prajānimittaṃ tvāṃ haniṣyāmi vasundhare yadi me vacanaṃ nādya kariṣyasi jagaddhitam  BndP tvāṃ nihatyāśu bāṇena macchāsanaparāṅmukhīm ātmānaṃ prathayitveha prajā dhārayitā svayam  BndP sā tvaṃ vacanamāsthāya mama dharmabhṛtāṃ vare saṃjīvaya prajā nityaṃ śaktā hyasi na saṃśayaḥ  BndP duhitṛtvaṃ ca me gaccha caivametamahaṃ śaram niyaccheyaṃ tvadvadhārthamudyantaṃ ghoradarśanam  BndP pratyuvāca tato vainyamevamuktā satī mahī sarvametadahaṃ rājanvidhāsyāmi na saṃśayaḥ  BndP vatsaṃ tu mama taṃ paśya kṣareyaṃ yena vatsalā samāṃ ca kuru sarvatra māṃ tvaṃ dharmmabhṛtāṃ vara yathā vispandamānaṃ me kṣīraṃ sarvatra bhāvayet  BndP sūta uvācatata utsārayāmāsa śilājālani sarvaśaḥ dhanuṣkoṭyā tathā vainyastena śailā vivarddhitāḥ  BndP manvantareṣvatīteṣu viṣamāsīdvasundharā svabhāvenā bhavattasyāḥ samāni viṣamāṇi ca  BndP na hi pūrvanisarge vai viṣame pṛthivītale pravibhāgaḥ purāṇāṃ vā grāmāṇāṃ vāpi vidyate  BndP na sasyāni na gorakṣaṃ na kṛṣirna vaṇikpathaḥ cākṣuṣasyāntare pūrvamāsīdetatpurā kila  BndP vaivasvateṃtare tasminsarva syaitasya saṃbhavaḥ samatvaṃ yatra yatrāsīdbhūmeḥ kasmiṃścideva hi  BndP tatra tatra prajāstā vai nivasaṃti ca sarvaśaḥ āhāraḥ phala mūle tu prajānāmabhavatkila  BndP kṛcchreṇaiva tadā tāsāmityevamanuśuśruma vainyātprabhṛti loke sminsarvasyaitasya saṃbhavaḥ  BndP sa kalpayitvā vatsaṃ tu cākṣuṣaṃ manumīśvaraḥ pṛthurdudoha sasyāni sve tale pṛthivīṃ tataḥ  BndP tenānnena tatastā vai varttayanti śubhāḥ prajāḥ ṛṣibhiḥ śrūyate cāpi punardugdhā vasuṃdharā  BndP vatsaḥ somastvabhūtteṣāṃ dogdhā cāpi bṛhaspatiḥ chandāsipātramāsīttu gāyatryādīni sarvaśaḥ  BndP kṣīramāsīttadā teṣāṃ tapo brahma ca śāśvatam punastato devagaṇaiḥ purandarapurogamaiḥ  BndP sauvarṇaṃ pātramādāya dugdhā saṃśrūyate mahī vatsastu maghavānāsīddogdhā ca savitā vibhuḥ  BndP kṣīramūrjaṃ ca madhu ca varttante tena devatāḥ pitṛbhiḥ śrūyate cāpi punardugdhā vasundharā  BndP rājataṃ pātramādāya svadhāmāśu vitṛptaye vaivasvato yamastvāsītteṣāṃ vatsaḥ pratāpavān  BndP antakaścābhavaddogdhā pitṝṇāṃ balavānprabhuḥ asuraiḥ śrūyate cāpi punardugdhā vasundharā  BndP āyasaṃ pātramādāya kila māyaśca sarvaśaḥ virocanastu prāhrādirvatsasteṣāṃ mahāyaśāḥ  BndP tratvigdvimūrddhā daityānāṃ dogdhābhūdditinandanaḥ pāyasā te ca māyābhiḥ sarve māyāvino surāḥ  BndP varttayanti mahāvīryāstadeṣāṃ paramaṃ balam nāgaistu śrūyate dugdhā vatsaṃ kṛtvā tu takṣakam  BndP alābapātramādāya viṣaṃ kṣīraṃ sumahāyaśāḥ tena te varttayantīti paramarthatayā ca ha  BndP rākṣasaiśca piśācaiśca punardugdhā vasundharā brahmā brāhyāstu vai dogadhā teṣāmāsītkuberakaḥ  BndP vatsaḥ sumālī balavānkṣīraṃ rudhirameva ca kapālapātre nirdugdhā hyantarddhanaṃ ca rākṣasaiḥ  BndP tena kṣīreṇa rakṣāṃsi varttayantīha sarvaśaḥ padmapātre punardugdhā gandharvaiścāpsa rogaṇaiḥ  BndP vatsaṃ citrarathaṃ kṛtvā śucīngandhāmahī vatsastu himavānāsīddogdhā merurmahāgiriḥ  BndP pātraṃ tu śailamevāsīttena śailāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ śrūyate vṛkṣavīrudbhiḥ punardugdhā vasundharā  BndP pālāśaṃ pātramādāya chinnadagdhaprarohaṇam kāmadhuk puṣpitaḥ śālaḥ plakṣo vatso yaśasvinām  BndP sarvakāmadughā dogdhrī pṛthivī bhūtabhāvinī saiva dhātrī vidhātrī ca dhāraṇī ca vasundharā  BndP dugdhā hitārthaṃ lokānāṃ pṛthuneti hi naḥ śrutam carācarasya lokasya pratiṣṭhā yonireva ca  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte pūrvabhāge dvitīye nuṣaṅga pāde śeṣamanvantarāśyānaṃ pṛthivīdohanaṃ ca nāma ṣaṭtriṃśattamo dhyāyaḥsūta uvācaāsīdiha samudrāntā vasudheti yathā śrutam vasu dhatte yatastasmādvasudhā seti gīyate  BndP madhukaiṭabhayoḥ pūrvaṃ medasā saṃpariplutā teneyaṃ medinītyuktā niruktyā brahmavādibhiḥ  BndP tato bhyupagamādrājñaḥ pṛthorvainyasya dhīmataḥ duhitṛtvamanuprāptā pṛthivī paṭhyate tataḥ  BndP pṛthunā pravibhāgaścadharāyāḥ sādhitaḥ purā tasyākaravatī rājñaḥ pattanākaramālinī  BndP cāturvarṇamayasamākīrṇā rakṣitā tena dhīmatā evaṃprabhāvorājāsīdvainyaḥ sadvijasattamāḥ  BndP namasyaścaiva pūcyaśca bhūtagrāmeṇa sarvaśaḥ brāhmaṇaiśca mahābhāgairvedavedāṅgapāragaiḥ  BndP pṛthureva namaskāryo brahmayoniḥ sanātanaḥ pārthivaiśca mahābhāgaiḥ prārthayadbhirmahadyaśaḥ  BndP ādirājo namaskāryaḥ pṛthurvainyaḥ pratāpavān yodhairapi ca saṃgrāme prāptukāmairjayaṃ yudhi  BndP ādikarttāraṇānāṃ vai namasyaḥ pṛthureva hi yo hi yoddhā raṇaṃ yāti kīrttayitvā pṛthuṃ nṛpam  BndP sa ghorarūpātsaṃgrāmātkṣemī tarati kīrttimān vaiśyairapi ca rājarṣirveśyavṛttimihāsthitaiḥ  BndP pṛthureva namaskāryo vṛttidānānmahāyaśāḥ ete vatsaviśeṣāśca dogdhāraḥ kṣīrameva ca  BndP pātrāṇi ca mayoktāni sarvāṇyeva yathākramam brahmaṇā prathamaṃ dugdhā purā pṛthvī mahātmanā  BndP vāyuṃ kṛtvā tathā vatsaṃ bījāni vasudhātale tataḥ svāyaṃbhuve pūrvaṃ tadā manvantare punaḥ  BndP vatsaṃ svāyaṃbhuvaṃ kṛtvā sarvasasyāni caiva hi tataḥ svārociṣe vāpi prāpte manvantare dhunā  BndP vatsaṃ svārociṣaṃ kṛtvā dugdhā sasyāni medinī uttamena tu tenāpi dugdhā devānu jena tu  BndP manuṃ kṛtvottamaṃ vatsaṃ sarvasasyāni dhīmatā punaśca pañcame pṛthvī tāmasasyāntare manoḥ  BndP dugdheyaṃ tāmasaṃ vatsaṃ kṛtvā vai balabandhunā cāriṣṭavasya vai ṣaṣṭhe saṃprāpte cāntare manoḥ  BndP dugdhā mahī purāṇena vatsaṃ cāriṣṭavaṃ prati cākṣuṣe cāpi saṃprāpte tadā manvantare punaḥ  BndP dugdhā mahī purāṇena vatsaṃ kṛtvā tu cākṣuṣam cākṣuṣasyāntare tīte prāpte vaivasvate punaḥ  BndP vainyeneyaṃ purā dugdhā yathā te kathitaṃ mayā etairdugdhā purā pṛthvī vyatīteṣvantareṣu vai  BndP devādibhirmanuṣyaiśca tato bhūtādibhiśca ha evaṃ sarveṣu vijñeyā atītānāgateṣviha  BndP devā manvantare svasthāḥ pṛthostu śṛṇuta prajāḥ pṛthostu putrau vikrāntau jajñāte ntarddhipāṣanau  BndP śikhaṇḍinī havirdhānamantarddhānāvdyajāyata havirdhānātṣaḍāgneyī dhiṣaṇājanayatsutān  BndP prācīnabarhiṣaṃ śuklaṃ gayaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ prajācinau prācīnabarhirbhagavānmahānāsītprajāpatiḥ  BndP balaśrutatapovīryaiḥ pṛthivyāmekarāḍasau prācīnāgrāḥ kuśāstasya tasmātprācīnabarhyasau  BndP samudratanayāyāṃ tu kṛtadāraḥ sa vai prabhuḥ mahatastapasaḥ pāre savarṇāyāṃ prajāpatiḥ  BndP savarṇādhatta sāmudrī daśa prācīnabarhiṣaḥ sarvānpracetaso nāma dhanurvedasya pāragān  BndP apṛthagdharmacaraṇāste tapyanta mahāttapaḥ daśavarṣa sahasrāṇi samudrasalileśayāḥ  BndP tapaścateṣu pṛthivīṃ tapyatsvatha mahīruhāḥ arakṣyamāṇāmāvabrurbabhūvātha prajākṣayaḥ  BndP pratyāhṛte tadā tasmiñcākṣuṣasyāntare manoḥ nāśakanmāruto vātuṃ vṛttaṃ khamabhavaddrumaiḥ  BndP daśavarṣasahasrāṇi na śekuśceṣṭituṃ prajāḥ tadupaśrutya tapasā sarve yuktāḥ pracetasaḥ  BndP mukhebhyo vāyumagniṃ ca sasṛjurjātamanyavaḥ unmūlānatha vṛkṣāṃstānkṛtvā vāyuraśoṣayat  BndP tānagniradahaddhora evamāsīddumakṣayaḥ drumakṣayamatho buddhvā kiñcicchiṣṭeṣu śākhiṣu  BndP upagamyābravī detānrājā somaḥ pracetasaḥ dṛṣṭvā prayojanaṃ satyaṃ lokasaṃtānakāraṇāt  BndP kopaṃ tyajata rājānaḥ sarve prācīnabarhiṣaḥ vṛkṣāḥ kṣityāṃ janiṣyanti śāmyatāmagnimārutau  BndP ratnabhūtā ca kanyeyaṃ vṛkṣāṇāṃ varavarṇinīḥ bhaviṣyajjanatā hyeṣā dhṛtā garbheṇa vai mayā  BndP māriṣā nāma nāmnaiṣā vṛkṣaireva vinirmitā bhāryā bhavatu vo hyeṣā somagarbhā vivarddhitā  BndP yuṣmākaṃ tejasārddhena mama cārdhena tejasā asyāmutpatsyate vidvāndakṣo nāma prajāpatiḥ  BndP sa imāṃ dagdhabhūyiṣṭhāṃ yuṣmattejomayena vai agnināgnisamo bhūyaḥ prajāḥ saṃvarddhayiṣyati  BndP tataḥ somasya vacanājjagṛhuste pracetasaḥ saṃtdṛtya kopaṃ vṛkṣebhyaḥ patnīṃ dharmeṇa māriṣām  BndP māriṣāyāṃ tataste vai manasā garbhamādadhuḥ daśabhyastu pracetobhyo māriṣāyāṃ prajāpatiḥ  BndP dakṣo jajñe mahātejāḥ somasyāṃśena vīryavān asṛjanmanasā tvādau prajā dakṣo tha maithunāt  BndP acarāṃśca carāṃścaiva dvipado tha catuṣpadaḥ visṛjya manasā dakṣaḥ paścādasṛjata striyaḥ  BndP dadau sa daśa dharmāya kaśyapāya trayāṃ daśa kālasya nayane yuktāḥ saptaviṃśatimindave  BndP ebhyo dattvā tato nyā vai catasro riṣṭanemine dve caiva bahuputrāya dve caivāṅgirase tathā  BndP kanyāmekāṃ kṛśāśvāya tebhyo patyaṃ babhūva ha antaraṃ cākṣuṣasyātha manoḥ ṣaṣṭhaṃ tu gīyate  BndP manorvaivasvatasyāpi saptamasya prajāpateḥ vasudevāḥ khagā gāvo nāgā ditijadānavāḥ  BndP gandharvāpsarasaścaiva jajñire nyāśca jātayaḥ tataḥ prabhṛti loke sminprajā maithunasaṃbhavāḥ saṃkalpāddarśanātsparśātpūrvāsāṃ sṛṣṭirucyate  BndP ṛṣiruvācadevānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca devarṣiṇāṃ ca te śubhaḥ saṃbhavaḥ kathitaḥ pūrvaṃ dakṣasya ca mahātmanaḥ  BndP prāṇātprajāpaterjanma dakṣasya kathitaṃ tvayā kathaṃ prāce tastvaṃ ca punarlebhe mahātapāḥ  BndP etaṃ naḥ saṃśayaṃ sūta vyākhyātuṃ tvamihārhasi dauhitraścaiva somasya kathaṃ śrvaśuratāṃ gataḥ  BndP sūta uvācautpattiśca nirodhaśca nityaṃ bhūteṣu sattamāḥ ṛṣayo tra na suhyanti vidyāvantaśca ye janāḥ  BndP yuge yuge bhavantyete sarve dakṣādayo dvijāḥ punaścaiva nirudhyante vidvāṃstatra na muhyati  BndP jyaiṣṭhyakāniṣṭhyamapyeṣāṃ pūrvamāsīddvijottamāḥ tapa eva garīyo bhūtprabhāvaścaiva kāraṇam  BndP imāṃ visṛṣṭiṃ yo veda cākṣuṣasya carācaram prajāvānāyuṣastīrṇaḥ svargaloke mahīyate  BndP evaṃ sargaḥ samākhyātaścākṣuṣasya samāsataḥ ityete ṣaṭ nisargāśca krāntā manvantarātmakāḥ  BndP svāyaṃbhuvādyāḥ saṃkṣepāccāśuṣāntā yathākramam ete sargā yathā prājñaiḥ proktā ye dvijasattamāḥ  BndP vaivasvatanisargeṇa teṣāṃ jñeyastu vistaraḥ anyūnānatiriktāste sarve sargā vivasvataḥ  BndP ārogyāyuḥ pramāṇebhyo dharmataḥ kāmatorthataḥ etāneva guṇāneti yaḥ paṭhannanasūyakaḥ  BndP vaivasvatasya vakṣyāmi sāṃpratasya mahātmanaḥ samāsavyāsataḥ sargaṃ bruvato me nibodhata  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte pūrvabhāge dvitīye nuṣaṅgapāde cākṣuṣasargavarṇanaṃ nāma saptatriṃśattamo dhyāyaḥsūta uvācasaptama tvatha paryāye manorvaivasvatasya ha mārīcātkaśyapāddevā jajñire paramarṣayaḥ  BndP ādityā vasavī rudrāḥ sādhyā viśve marudgaṇāḥ bhṛgavoṃgirasaścaiva te ṣṭhau devagaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ  BndP ādityā maruto rudrā vijñeyāḥ kaśyapātmajāḥ sādhyāśya vasavo viśve dharmaputrāstrayo gaṇāḥ  BndP bhṛgostu bhṛgavo devā hyaṅgirasoṃgiraḥ sutāḥ vaivasvateṃtare hyasminnitye te chandajā matāḥ  BndP ete pi ca gamiṣyanti mahāntaṃ kālaparyayāt evaṃ sargastu mārīco vijñeyaḥ sāṃprataḥ śubhaḥ  BndP tejasvī sāṃpratasteṣāmindro nāmnā mahābalaḥ atītānāgatā ye ca varttante sāṃprataṃ ca ye  BndP sarve manvantaredrāste vijñeyāstulyalakṣaṇāḥ bhūtabhavyabhavannāthāḥ sahasrākṣāḥ purandarāḥ  BndP saghavantaścate sarve śṛṅgiṇo vajrapāṇayaḥ sarvaiḥ kratuśateneṣṭaṃ pṛthakchataguṇena tu  BndP trailokye yāni sattvāni gatimanti dhruvāṇi ca abhibhūyāvatiṣṭhanti dharmādyaiḥ kāraṇairapi  BndP tejasā tapasā buddhyā balaśrutaparākramaiḥ bhūtabhavyabhavannāthā yathā te prabhaviṣṇavaḥ  BndP etatsarvaṃ pravakṣyāmi bruvato me nibodhata bhūtabhavyabhavaddhyeta tsamṛtaṃ lokatrayaṃ dvijaiḥ  BndP bhūrloko yaṃ smṛto bhūtamantarikṣaṃ bhavatsmṛtam bhavyaṃ smṛtaṃ divaṃ hyetatteṣāṃ vakṣyāmi sādhanam  BndP dhyāyatā lokanāmāni brahmaṇāgre vibhāṣitam bhūriti vyāhṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ bhūrloko yamabhūttadā  BndP bhū sattāyāṃ smṛto dhātustathāsau lokadarśane bhūtatvāddarśanāccaiva bhūrloko yamabhūttataḥ  BndP ato yaṃ prathamo loko bhūtatvādbhūrdvajaiḥ smṛtaḥ bhūte sminbhavadityuktaṃ dvitīyaṃ brahmaṇā punaḥ  BndP bhavadityatpadyamāne kāle śabdo yamucyate bhavanāttu bhuvalloko niruttayā hi nirucyate  BndP antarikṣaṃ bhavattasmāddvitīyo loka ucyate utpanne tu tathā loke dvitīye brahmaṇā punaḥ  BndP bhavyeti vyāhṛtaṃ paścādbhavyo lokastato bhavat anāgate bhavya ita śabda eṣa vibhāvyate  BndP tasmādbhavyo hyasau loko nāmatastridivaṃ smṛtam bhūritīyaṃ smṛtā bhūmirantarikṣaṃ bhuvaḥ smṛtam  BndP divaṃ smṛtaṃ tathā bhavyaṃ tralokyasyaiṣa nirṇayaḥ trailokyayuktairvyāhāraistisro vyāhṛtayo bhavan  BndP nātha ityeṣa dhāturvai dhātujñaiḥ pālane smṛtaḥ yasmādbhūtasya lokasya bhavyasya bhavatastathā  BndP lokatrayasya nāthāste tasmādindrādvijaiḥ smṛtāḥ pradhānabhūtā devendrā guṇabhūtāstathaiva ca  BndP manvantareṣu ye devā yajñabhājo bhavanti hi yajñagandharvarakṣāṃsi piśāco ragamānuṣāḥ  BndP mahimānaḥ smṛtā hyete devendrāṇāṃ tu sarvaśaḥ devendrā guravo nāthā rājānaḥ pitaro hi te  BndP rakṣantīmāḥ prajā hyete dharmeṇeha surottamāḥ ityetallakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ devendrāṇāṃ samāsataḥ  BndP saptarṣīnsaṃpravakṣyāmi sāṃprataṃ ye divaṃ śritāḥ gādhijaḥ kauśiko dhīmānviśvāmitro mahātapāḥ  BndP bhārgavo jamadagniśca hyaurvaputraḥ pratāpavān bṛhaspatisutaścāpi bharadvājo mahā yaśāḥ  BndP autathyo gautamo vidvāñśaradvānnāma dhārmikaḥ svāyaṃbhuvo trirbhagavānbrahmakośaḥ sapañcamaḥ  BndP ṣaṣṭho vasiṣṭhaputrastu vasumāṃllokaviśrutaḥ vatsaraḥ kāśyapaśyaiva saptaite sādhusaṃmatāḥ  BndP ete saptarṣayaśyoktā varttante sāṃprateṃtare ikṣvākuśca nṛgaścaiva dhṛṣṭaḥ śaryātireba ca  BndP nariṣyantaścavikhyāto nābhāgo diṣṭa eva ca karūṣaśca pṛṣadhraśca pāṃśuścanavamaḥ smṛtaḥ  BndP manorvaivasvatasyaite nava putrāḥ sudhārmikāḥ kīrtitā vai tathā hyete saptamaṃ caitadantaram  BndP ityeṣa ha mayā pādo dvitīyaḥ kathitodvijāḥ vistareṇānupūrvyā ca bhūyaḥ kiṃ kathayāmyaham  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte pūrvabhāge dvitīye nuṣaṅgapāde manvantaravarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭātriṃśattamo dhyāyaḥsamāpto yaṃ brahmāṇḍamahāpurāṇapūrvabhāgaḥ
